śivena eva tasmāt te vijayaḥ sadā anumene ca tad vākyam bhaṇḍaḥ dānava nāyakaḥ tapas vighna karān dṛṣṭvā dānavān jagadambikā tam dṛṣṭvā dānava indraḥ api kim etat iti vismitaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ dānava astreṇa babhañja atibalena tu vāyavya astreṇa tam dhīraḥ babhañja ca nanāda ca etat dṛṣṭvā tu daitya indraḥ viṣaṇmaḥ sva puram yayau tām ca dṛṣṭvā jagaddhātrīm dṛṣṭvā prākāram ujjvalam tān uvāca tatas śakraḥ daitya indraḥ ayam iha āgataḥ kuṇḍam yojana vistāram samyak kṛtvā tu śobhanam mahā yāga vidhānena praṇidhāya hutāśanam yajāmaḥ paramām śāktim mahā māsaiḥ vayam surāḥ brahma bhūtāḥ bhaviṣyāmaḥ bhokṣyāmaḥ vā triviṣṭapam huteṣu sarva māṃseṣu pādeṣu ca kareṣu ca jagat ujjīvana karīm brahma viṣṇu śiva ātmakām saundarya sāra sīmām tām ānanda rasa sāgarām japā kusuma saṃkāśām dāḍima kusuma ambarām sarva ābharaṇa saṃyuktām śṛṅgāra eka rasa ālayām taraṃgita apāṅga nayana āloka kaumudīm pāśa aṅkuśa ikṣu kodaṇḍa pañcabāṇa lasat karām tām vilokya mahādevīm devāḥ sarve sa vāsavāḥ praṇemuḥ mudita ātmānaḥ bhūyas bhūyas akhila ātmikam saṃpūrṇa aṅgāḥ dṛḍhatarāḥ vajra dehāḥ mahā balāḥ tuṣṭuvuḥ ca mahā devīm ambikām akhila artha dām iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitopākhyāne lalitāprādurbhāvaḥ nāma dvādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ūcuḥ ca vāma akṣe jaya kāri ca vāma akṣe jaya kāmākṣi sundari jaya ji akhila sura ārādhye jaya kāmeśi mānade jaya nārāyaṇi pare nandita aśeṣa viṣṭape jaya śrīkaṇṭha dayite jaya śrī lalitā iṃbike jātasya jāyamānasya iṣṭāpūrtasya hetave kalā muhūrta kāṣṭha ahar māsa ṛtu śarad ātmane rasātalam kaṭi deśaḥ kukṣiḥ te dharaṇī bhavet dṛśaḥ candra arka dahanāḥ diśaḥ te bāhavaḥ oṃbike marutaḥ tu tava ucchvāsāḥ vācaḥ te śrutayaḥ akhilāḥ krīḍā te loka racanā sakhā te cit mayaḥ śivaḥ māhāraḥ te sadānandaḥ vāsaḥ te hṛdaye satām dṛśya adṛśya svarūpāṇi rūpāṇi bhuvanāni te śiroruhāḥ ghanāḥ te tu tārakāḥ kusumāni te yamāḥ ca niyamāḥ ca eva kara pāda ruhāḥ tathā prāṇāyāmaḥ tu te nāsā rasanā te sarasvatī pratyāhāraḥ tu idriṃyāṇi dhyānam te dhī tu sattamā manaḥ te dhāraṇā śaktiḥ hṛdayam te samādhikaḥ mahīruhāḥ te iṅgaruhāḥ prabhātam vasanam tava yajñarūpā jagaddhātrī viśvarūpā ca pāvanī ādau yā tu dayā bhūtā sasarja nikhilāḥ prajāḥ hṛdaya sthā api lokānām adṛśyā mohana ātmakā nāma rūpa vibhāgam ca yā karoti sva līlayā tāni adhiṣṭhāya tiṣṭhantī teṣu asakta artha kāma dā yad ājñayā pravartante vahni sūrya edumārutāḥ pṛthivī ādīni bhūtāni tasyai devyai namaḥ namaḥ yā sasarja ādidhātāram sarga ādau ādi bhūri dam yathā dhṛtā tu dhariṇī yayā ākāśam ameyayā arūpam advandvam adṛṣṭa gocaram prabhāvam agryam katham amba varṇaye iti statvā mahādevīm devāḥ sarve sa vāsavāḥ bhūyas bhūyas namaskṛtya śaraṇam jagamuḥ añjasā tatas prasannā sā devī praṇatam vīkṣya vāsavam yadi tuṣṭā asi karyāṇi varam daitya indra pīḍitaḥ durdharam jīvitam dehi tvām gatāḥ śaraṇa arthinaḥ uvāca nirbhayāḥ muditāḥ santu sarve deva gaṇāḥ tathā ye stoṣyanti ca mām bhaktyā stavena anena mānavāḥ bhājanam te bhaviṣyanti dharma śrī yaśasām sadā vidyā vinaya saṃpannāḥ nīrogāḥ dīrgha jīvinaḥ modam paramam jagmuḥ tām vilokya muhur muhur iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitopākhyāne lalitāstavarājaḥ nāma trayodaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ ājagāma atha deveśīm draṣṭu kāmaḥ mahā ṛṣibhiḥ ājagāma tatas viṣṇuḥ ārūḍhaḥ vinatā sutam mad api vṛṣam ārūḍhaḥ samāyātaḥ akhila īśvarām devarṣayaḥ nārada ādyāḥ samājagmuḥ maheśvarīm āyayuḥ tām mahā devīm sarve ca apsarasām gaṇāḥ viśvāvasu prabhṛtayaḥ gandharvāḥ ca eva yakṣakāḥ brahmaṇā atha samādiṣṭaḥ viśvakarmā viśām patiḥ cakāra nagaram divyam yathā amarapuram tathā vidyā adhidevatā śyāmā samājagmatuḥ aṃbikām mātaraḥ ca eva sva sva bhūta gaṇa āvṛtāḥ siddhayaḥ hi aṇima ādyāḥ ca yoginyaḥ ca eva koṭiśas bhairavāḥ kṣetrapālāḥ ca mahā śāstāḥ gaṇāgraṇī mahā gaṇeśvaraḥ skandaḥ baṭukaḥ vīrabhadrakaḥ āgatya te mahādevīm tuṣṭuvuḥ praṇatāḥ tadā tatra atha nagarīm ramyām sa aṭṭa prākāra toraṇām gaja aśva ratha śālā āḍhyām rāja vīthi virājitām sāmantānām amātyānām sainikānām dvijanma nām vetāla dāsa dāsīnām gṛhāni rucirāṇi ca madhyam rājagṛham divyam dvāra gopura bhūṣitam śālābhiḥ bahubhiḥ yuktam sabhābhiḥ uṣa śobhitam siṃhāsana sabhām ca eva nava ratna mayīm śubhām madhye siṃhāsanam divyam yaḥ tu etat samadhiṣṭhāya vartate bāliśaḥ api vā na kevalā strī rājya arhā puruṣaḥ api tayā vinā maṅgala ācārya saṃyuktam mahāpuruṣa lakṣaṇam anukūla aṅganā yuktam abhiṣiñcet iti śrutiḥ vibhāti iyam varārohā bhūrtā śṛṅgāradevatā varaḥ asyāḥ triṣu lokeṣu na ca anyaḥ śaṃkarāt ṛte muṇḍadhārī ca virūpākṣaḥ kapālabhṛt bhasma digdha aṅgaḥ śmaśāna asthi vibhūṣaṇaḥ amaṅgala āspadam ca enam varayet sā su maṅgalā koṭi kandarpa lāvaṇya yuktaḥ divya śarīravān kirīṭa hāra keyūra kuṇḍala ādyaiḥ alaṅkṛtaḥ tam kumāram atha āliṅgya brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ cakre kāmeśvaram nāmnā kamanīya vapus dharam astuvan te parām śaktim brahma viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ tām dṛṣṭvā mṛgaśāvākṣīm kumāraḥ nīlalohitaḥ abhavat manmatha āviṣṭaḥ vismṛtya sakalāḥ kriyāḥ sā api tam vīkṣya tanu aṅgaḥ mūrtiṃmantam iva smaram madana āviṣṭa sarva aṅgī sva ātma rūpam amanyata atha uvāca mahādevīm brahmā loka eka nāyikām ime devāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ gandharva apsarasām gaṇāḥ tvām īśām draṣṭum icchanti sa priyām parama āhave loka saṃrakṣaṇa arthāya bhajasva puruṣam param rājñī bhava purasya asya sthitā bhava varāsane abhiṣiktām mahābhāgaiḥ devārṣe bhiḥ akalmaṣaiḥ sāmrājya cihna saṃyuktām sarva ābharaṇa saṃyutām sa priyām āsana gatām draṣṭum icchāmahe vayam iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne madanakāmeśvaraprādurbhāvaḥ nāma caturdaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ uvāca saḥ tatas vākyam brahma viṣṇu mukhān surān svatantrā aham sadā devāḥ sva icchā ācāra vihāriṇī uvāca ca mahādevīm dharma artha sahitam vacaḥ kāla krītā kraya krītā pitṛ dattā svayaṃyutā tu veśyā syāt kraya krītā tu dāsikā gandharva udvāhitā yuktā bhāryā syāt pitṛdattakā samāna dharmiṇī yuktā bhāryā pitṛ vaśaṃvadā cit ānanda ātmakam tasmāt prakṛtiḥ samajāyata tvam eva anādiḥ akhilā kārya kāraṇa rūpiṇī tvām eva hi praśaṃsanti pañca brahma svarūpiṇīm tvām eva hi sṛjasi ādau tvam eva hi avasi kṣaṇāt bhajasva puruṣam kañcid loka anugraha kāmyayā iti vijñāpitā devī brahmaṇā sakalaiḥ suraiḥ tayā utsṛṣṭā hi sā mālā śobhayantī nabhasthalam papāta kaṇṭha deśe hi tadā kāmeśvarasya tu vavṛṣuḥ puṣpa varṣāṇi manda vāta īritāḥ ghanāḥ tvad rūpā hi mahādevī sahajaḥ ca bhavān api dātum arhasi kalyāṇīm asmai kāmaśivāya tu dadau tasyai vidhānena prītyā tām śaṅkarāya tu deva ṛṣi pitṛ mukhyānām sarveṣām deva yoginām kalyāṇam kārayāmāsa śivayoḥ ādikeśavaḥ upāyanāni pradaduḥ sarve brahma ādayaḥ surāḥ tayoḥ puṣpāyudham prādāt amlānam hariḥ avyayam nāgapāśam dadau tābhyām varuṇaḥ yādasāṃpatiḥ aṅkuśam ca dadau tābhyām viśvakarmā viśām patiḥ prāyacchat tāṭaṅkau candra bhāskarau nava ratna mayām bhūṣām prādāt ratnākaraḥ svayam dadau surāṇām adhipaḥ madhu pātram atha akṣayam cintāmaṇi mayīm mālām kuberaḥ pradadau tadā sāmrājya sūcakam chatram dadau lakṣmīpatiḥ svayam gaṅgā ca yamunā tābhyām ca amare candra bhāsvare aṣṭau ca vasavaḥ rudrāḥ ādityāḥ ca aśvinaḥ tathā dikpālāḥ marutaḥ sādhyāḥ gandharvāḥ pramatha īśvarāḥ svāni svāni āyudhāni asyai pradaduḥ paritoṣitāḥ rathān ca turagān nāgān mahā vegān mahā balān uṣṭān arogān aśvān tān kṣudh tṛṣṇā parivarjitān daduḥ vajra upama ākārān sa āyudhān sa paricchadān atha abhiṣekam ātenuḥ sāmrājye śivayoḥ śivam atha akarot vimānam ca nāmnā tu kusumākaram vidhātā a mlāna mālam vai nityam ca abhedyam āyudhaiḥ yat gandha ghrāṇa mātreṇa bhrānti roga kṣurdhātayaḥ tad kṣaṇāt eva naśyanti manaḥ hlāda karam śubham vīṇā veṇu mṛdaṅga ādi vividhaiḥ taurya vādanaiḥ yayau vīthim vihāra īśā śobhayantī nija ojasā sa lāja akṣata hastābhiḥ purandhrībhiḥ ca varṣitā gāthābhiḥ maṅgala arthābhiḥ vīṇā veṇu ādini svanaiḥ tuṣyantī vīvīthi vīthīṣu manda mandam atha āyayau pratigṛhya apsa robhiḥ tu kṛtam nīrājana vidhim siṃhāsanam adhiṣṭhāya saha devena śaṃbhunā sarvajñā sa akṣipātena tad tad kāmān apūrayat tat dṛṣṭvā caritam devyāḥ brahmā loka pitāmahaḥ kāmākṣī iti tadā abhikhyām dadau kāmeśvarī iti ca vavarṣa āścarya meghaḥ api pure tasmin tad ājñayā mahārhāni ca vastūni divyāni ābharaṇāni ca cintāmaṇiḥ kalpavṛkṣaḥ kamalā kāmadhenavaḥ tām sevā eka rasa ākārām vimukta anya kriyā guṇāḥ sarva kāma artha saṃyuktāḥ hṛṣyantaḥ sārvakālikam pitāmahaḥ hariḥ ca eva mahādevaḥ ca vāsavaḥ anye diśām adhīśāḥ tu sakalāḥ devatā gaṇāḥ devarṣayaḥ nārada ādyāḥ sanaka ādyāḥ ca yoginaḥ mahā ṛṣayaḥ ca manu ādyāḥ vasiṣṭha ādyāḥ tapodhanāḥ gandharva apsarasaḥ yakṣāḥ yāḥ ca anyāḥ deva jātayaḥ divi bhūmi antarikṣeṣu sa saṃbādham vasaṃti ye toṣayāmāsa satatam anurāgeṇa bhūyasā rājñaḥ mahati bhūrloke viduṣaḥ sakala īpsitām rājñī dudoha abhīṣṭāni sarva bhū tala vāsinām triloka eka mahīpāle sa ambike kāma śaṅkare daśa varṣa sahasrāṇi yayuḥ kṣaṇaḥ iva aparaḥ tatas kadā cit āgatya nāradaḥ bhagavān ṛṣiḥ praṇamya paramām śaktim provāca vinaya anvitaḥ asat jana vināśa arthā sat jana abhyudaya arthinī pravṛttiḥ te kalyāṇe sādhūnām rakṣaṇāya hi ayam bhaṇḍaḥ asuraḥ devi bādhate jagatām trayam tvad sevā eka parāḥ devāḥ cira kālam iha uṣitāḥ tvad ājñayā gamiṣyanti svāni svāni purāṇi tu amaṅgalāni śūnyāni samṛddha arthāni saṃtvataḥ evam vijñāpitā devī nāradena akhila īśvarā sva sva vāsa nivāsāya preṣayāmāsa ca amarān brahmāṇam ca harim śambhum vāsava ādīn diśām patīn yathārham pūjayitvā tu preṣayāmāsa ca ambikā aparādham tatas tyaktum api saṃpreṣitāḥ surāḥ sva sva aṃśaiḥ śivayoḥ sevām ādi pitroḥ akurvata etat ākhyānam āyuṣyam sarva maṅgala kāraṇam bhāvam mahādevyāḥ tasyāḥ rājya abhiṣecanam yaśaḥ prāpnoti vipulam samāna uttama tām api tāpa traya vihīnaḥ ca puruṣa arthaiḥ ca pūryate trisaṃdhyam yaḥ japet nityam dhyātvā siṃhāsana īśvarām ṣaṣ māsāt mahatīm lakṣmīm prāpnuyāt jāpaka uttamaḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne vaivāhikotsavaḥ nāma pañcadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha sā jagatām mātā lalitā parameśvarī trailokya kaṇṭakam bhaṇḍam daityam jetum viniryayau cakāra mardala ākārān ambhaḥ rāśīn tu sapta te prabhūta mardala dhvānaiḥ pūrayāmāsuḥ ambaram mṛdaṅga murajāḥ ca eva paṭahaḥ selukā jhallarī rāṅghā huhukā huṇḍukā ghaṭāḥ paṇavāḥ ca eva gomukhāḥ ca ardhacandrikāḥ yava madhyāḥ muṣṭi madhyāḥ marddala aḍiṇḍimāḥ api barītāḥ ca iṅgya āliṅgya prabheda jāḥ uddhakāḥ caituhuṇḍāḥ ca niḥsāṇāḥ barbarāḥ pare huṅkārā kākatuṇḍāḥ ca vādya bhedāḥ tathā apare dadhvanuḥ śakti senābhiḥ āhatāḥ samara udyame lalitā parameśānyāḥ aṅkuśa astrāt samudgatā saṃpatkarī nāma devī cacāla saha śaktibhiḥ aneka koṭi mātaṅga turaṃga ratha paṅktibhiḥ sevitā taruṇa ādityapāṭalā saṃpad īśvarā raṇa kolāhalam nāma sā āruroha mataṃga jam tām anvagāḥ yayau senā mahatī dhora rāviṇī lolābhiḥ ketumālābhiḥ ullikhatī dhana adhanāt tasyāḥ ca saṃpad nāthāyāḥ pīna stana su saṃkaṭaḥ kaṇṭakaḥ ghana saṃnāhaḥ ruruce vakṣasi sthitaḥ kaṃpamānā khaḍga latā vyarucat tad kare dhṛtā kuṭilā kālanāthasya bhṛkuṭī iva bhayaṅkarā utpāta vāta saṃpātāt calitāḥ iva parvatāḥ tām anvagāḥ yayuḥ koṭi saṃkhyākāḥ kuñjara uttamāḥ atha śrī lalitā devyā śrī pāśa āyudha saṃbhavā ati tvarita vikrāntiḥ aśva ārūḍha acalat puras tayā saha haya prāyam sainyam heṣā taraṅgitam vanāyu jāḥ ca kāṃbojāḥ pāradāḥ sindhu deśa jāḥ ṭaṅkaṇāḥ parvatīyāḥ ca pārasīkāḥ tathā pare ajāneyāḥ ghaṭṭadharāḥ daradāḥ kāla vandijāḥ vālmīka yāvana udbhūtāḥ gāndharvāḥ ca atha ye hayāḥ prāñc deśa jātāḥ kairātā prānta deśa udbhavāḥ tathā vinītāḥ sādhu voḍhāraḥ veginaḥ sthira cetasaḥ svāmi citta viśeṣa jñāḥ mahā yuddha sahiṣṇavaḥ lakṣaṇaiḥ bahuṣu yuktāḥ jita krodhāḥ jita śramāḥ pañca dhārāsu śakṣa ḍhyāḥ vinītāḥ ca plava anvitāḥ phala śukti śriyā yuktāḥ śveta śukti samanvitāḥ atha svastika śuktiḥ ca gaḍuram puṣpa gaṇḍikām etāni śubha lakṣmāṇi jyā rājya pradāni ca hantaḥ vāta javanāḥ vājinaḥ tām samanvayuḥ sthūla vāladhi vikṣepa kṣipyamāṇa payodharam jaṅghā kāṇḍa samunnaddha maṇi kiṅkiṇī bhāsuram mādayantam iva uccaṇḍaiḥ khura niṣṭhura kuṭṭanaiḥ bhū maṇḍala mahā vādyam vijayasya samṛddhaye ghoṣamāṇam prati muhur saṃdarśita gati kramam ālola cāmara vyājāt vahantam pakṣatī iva bhāṇḍaiḥ manoharaiḥ yuktam ghargharī jāla maṇḍitam eṣām ghoṣasya kapaṭāt huṃkurvatī imi vā asurān aśva ārūḍhā mahā devī samārūḍhā hayam yayau caturbhiḥ vāhubhiḥ pāśam aṅkuśam vetram eva ca taruṇa āditya saṅkāśā jvalat kāñcī taraṃgiṇī sañcacāla haya ārūḍhā nartayatī iva vājinam atha śrī daṇḍanāthāyāḥ niryāṇa paṭaha dhvaniḥ uddaṇḍa sindhu nisvānaḥ cakāra badhiram jagat vajra bāṇaiḥ kaṭhoraiḥ ca bhindantyaḥ kakubhaḥ daśa anyuddhata bhuja aśmānaḥ śaktayaḥ kāścid ucchritāḥ kāścid śrī daṇḍanāthāyāḥ khaḍgam phalakam ādāya pupluvuḥ caṇḍa saktayaḥ atyanta sainya sambādham vetra saṃtāḍanaiḥ śataiḥ atha tuṅga dhvaja śreṇīḥ mahiṣa aṅkāḥ mṛgāṅkikām siha aṅkāḥ ca eva bibhrāṇāḥ śaktayaḥ vyacalan purā tatas śrī daṇḍanāthāyāḥ śveta chatram sahasraśas sphurat karāḥ pracalitāḥ śaktayaḥ kāścid ādaduḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne sasenavijayayātrā nāma ṣoḍaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ daṇḍanāthā viniryāṇe saṃkhyā atītaiḥ sita prabhaiḥ chattraiḥ gaganam āreje niḥsaṃkhyā śaśi maṇḍitam timiram nunude bhūyas tad kāṇḍamaṇi rociṣā vajra prabhā adhaga dhaga chāyā pūrita diṅmukhāḥ tālavṛntāḥ śatavidhāḥ kroḍa mukhyāḥ bale acalan caṇḍaḥ daṇḍa ādayaḥ tīvrā bhairavāḥ śula pāṇayaḥ jvalat keśā piśaṅga ābhāḥ taḍit bhāsura diṅmukhāḥ dahatyaḥ iva daitya oghān tīkṣṇaiḥ mārgaṇa vahnibhiḥ praceluḥ daṇḍanāthāyāḥ senāḥ nāsīra dhāvitāḥ atha potrī mukhī devī samāna ākṛti bhūṣaṇāḥ tad samāna āyudha karāḥ tad samāna sva vāhanāḥ tīkṣma daṃṣṭa viniṣṭhyūta vahri dhūma amita ambarāḥ tamāla śyāmala ākārāḥ kapilāḥ krūra locanāḥ sahasra mahiṣa ārūḍhāḥ praceluḥ sūkara ānanāḥ atha śrī daṇḍanāthā ca kari cakra ratha uttamāt vajraghoṣaḥ iti khyātam dhūta kesara maṇḍalam vyakta āsyam vikaṭa ākāram viśaṅkaṭa vilocanam daṃṣṭra kaṭakaṭatkāra badhirīkṛta diś taṭam bhū cakram āpātālam nimajjibhiḥ siṃhavāhanam āruhya vyacalat daṇḍanāyikā tasyām asura saṃhāre pravṛttāyām jvalat krudhi kim asau dhakṣyati ruṣā viśvam adya eva potriṇī kim vā musala ghātena bhūmim dvedhā kariṣyati atha vā hala nirghātaiḥ kṣobhayiṣyati vāridhīn iti trasta hṛdaḥ sarve gagane nākinām gaṇāḥ dūra adrutam vimānaiḥ ca sa trāsam dadṛśuḥ gatāḥ vavandire ca tāḥ devāḥ baddhāñjali puṭa anvitāḥ kāni dvādaśa nāmāni tasyāḥ devyāḥ vada prabho aśva ānana mahā prājña yeṣu me kautukam mahat śṛṇu dvādaśa nāmāni tasyāḥ devyāḥ ghaṭodbhava yad ākarṇana mātreṇa prasannā sā bhaviṣyati pañcamā daṇḍanāthā ca saṃketā samayeśvarī tathā samayasaṃketā vārāhī potriṇī tathā mahāsenā api ājñā cakreśvarī tathā arighnī ca iti samproktam nāma dvādaśakam mune saṃkaṭe duḥkham āpnoti na kadācana mānavaḥ etaiḥ nāmabhiḥ abhra sthāḥ saṃketām bahu tuṣṭuvuḥ teṣām anugraha arthāya pracacāla ca sā punar atha saṃketayoginyā mantranāthā pada spṛśaḥ niryāṇa sūcana karā divi dadhvāna kāhalī śṛṅgāra prāya bhūṣāṇām śārdūla śyāmala tviṣām vīṇā saṃyata pāṇīnām śaktīnām niryayau balam kāḥ cat gāyanti nṛtyanti matta kokila niḥsvanāḥ vīṇā veṇu mṛdaṅga ādyāḥ savilāsa padakramāḥ praceluḥ śaktayaḥ śyāmāḥ harṣayantyaḥ jagat janān mayūra vāhanāḥ kāścid katicid haṃsa vāhanāḥ katicid nakula ārūḍhāḥ katicid kokila āsanāḥ sarvāḥ ca śyāmala ākārāḥ kāścid karṇīratha sthitāḥ kādamba madhu mattāḥ ca kāścid ārūḍha saindhavāḥ mantranāthām puraskṛtya saṃpraceluḥ puras puras bāla arka varṇa kavacā mada ālola vilocanā prekṣayatī kaṭākṣa odhauḥ kiñcid bhrū vallī tāṇḍavaiḥ āsām madhye na ca anyāsām śaktīnām ujjvala udayā nirjagāma ghana śyāma śyāmalā mantranāyikā tām tuṣṭuvuḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ nāmabhiḥ nāka vāsinaḥ tāni ṣoḍaśa nāmāni śṛṇu kumbha samudbhavaiḥ saṃgītayoginī śyāmā śyāmalā mantranāyikā mantriṇī saciva īśī ca pradhāna īśī śukapriyā vīṇāvatī vaiṇikī ca mudriṇī priyakapriyā nipapriyā kadamba īśā kadamba vana vāsinī ca nāmāni ṣoḍaśa etāni kumbha ja etaiḥ yaḥ saciva īśānīm sakṛt stauti śarīravān rājya carcā tu yāvatī śaktīnām api carcā yā sā sarvatra jaya pradā atha saṃgīta yoginyāḥ kara sthāt śu kapotakāt namaskṛtya pradhāna īśīm idam āha sa bhaktimān catrajīvam imam nāma kodaṇḍam su mahattaram gṛhāṇa jagatām aṃba dānavānām nibarhaṇam imau ca akṣaya bāṇa āḍhyau tūṇīrau svarṇa citritau gṛhāṇa daitya nāśāya mama anugraha hetave arpitān cāpa tūṇīrān jagrāha priyaka priyā citrajīvam mahā cāpam ādāya ca śūkapriyā maurvīm udvādya bhūriśas saṃgīta yoginī cāpa dhvaninā pūritam jagat manasā nāka ālayānām ca manasā yana ānanda saṃpadā yantriṇī ca iti dve tasyāḥ paricārike śukam vīṇām ca sahasā vahatyau pariceratuḥ ālola valaya kvāṇa vardhiṣṇu guṇa nisvanam dhārayantī ghanaśyāmā cakāra ati manoharam citrajīva śarāseṇa bhūṣitā gītayoginī kālī kaṭākṣa vat tīkṣṇaḥ nṛtyat bhujaga bhīṣaṇaḥ ullasan dakṣiṇe pāṇau vilalāsa śilīmukhaḥ tām paścāt ca siṣevire tadvat śyāmala śobhā āḍhyāḥ devyaḥ bāṇa dhanus dharāḥ sahasra akṣauhiṇī saṃkhyāḥ tīvra vegāḥ mada alasāḥ āpūrayatyaḥ kakubham kalaiḥ kilikilā ravaiḥ iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne daṇḍanāthāśyāmalāsenāyātrā nāma saptadaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha rāja nāyikā śritā ājvalita aṅkuśā phaṇi samāna pāśa bhṛt daśa yojana āyati mātā jagat trayīm abhivṛṇvatā viśada mauktika ātmanā dhavala atapatra valayena bhāsurā śaśi maṇḍalasya sakhī tām upeyivasā abhivījitā ca maṇi kānta śobhinā vijaya ādi mukhya paricārikā gaṇaiḥ śaktyā eka rājya padavīm abhisūcayantī sāmrājya cihna śata maṇḍita sainya deśā saṃgīta vādya racanā abhiratha amarīṇām saṃstūyamāna vibhavā viśada prakāśā mad bhakti vipula añjali śekharāṇām ārāt ahaṃprathamikā kṛta sevanānām brahma īśa viṣṇu vṛṣa mukhya sura uttamānām kaṭākṣayantī kāmeśvarī prabhṛtibhiḥ kamanīya bhābhiḥ saṃgrāma veṣa racanā su manoharābhiḥ tīvrābhiḥ rāvaṇa suśakti paramparabhiḥ yuktam ratham samara karmaṇi cālayantī prodyat piśaṅga ruci bhāga mala aṃśukena vīta amanohara ruciḥ samare vyabhāsīt pañca adhikaiḥ viśati nāma ratnaiḥ prapañca pāpa praśama ati dakṣaiḥ saṃstūyamānā lalitā marudbhiḥ saṃgrāmam uddiśya samuccacāla vīji vaktra mahābuddhe pañcaviṃśati nāmabhiḥ lalitā parameśānyāḥ dehi karṇa rasāyanam parāṅkuśā sundarī cakranāthā ca sāmrājī cakriṇī tathā cakreśvarī mahādevī kāmeśī parameśvarī mahāvidyā śivā anaṅgavallabhā sarvapāṭalā kula nāthā āmnāya nāthā sarva āmnāya nivāsinī śṛṅgāranāyikā ca iti pañcaviṃśati nāmabhiḥ stuvanti ye mahābhāgām lalitām parameśvarīm te prāpnuvanti saubhāgyam aṣṭau siddhīḥ mahat yaśaḥ ittham pracaṇḍa saṃrambham cālayantī mahat balam bhaṇḍāsuram prati kruddhā cacāla lalitā ambikā iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne lalitā parameśvarī senā jaya yātrā nāma aṣṭādaśaḥ adhyāyaḥ cakrarāja ratha indrasya yāḥ parvaṇi samāśritāḥ devatāḥ prakaṭa abhikhyāḥ tāsām ākhyām nivedaya saṃkhyāḥ ca tāsām akhilāḥ varṇa bhedān ca śobhanān proktā siddhidevyaḥ tāsām nāmāni mat śṛṇu aṇimā mahimā ca eva laghimā garimā tathā bhāva vaśitā ca eva prāptiḥ siddhiḥ ca saptamā prākāmya mukti siddhiḥ ca sarvakāma abhidhā parā etā devyaḥ catur bāhavaḥ japā kusuma saṃnibhāḥ cintāmaṇi kapālam ca triśūlam siddhi kajjalam dadhānāḥ dayayā pūrṇāḥ yogibhiḥ ca niṣevitāḥ tatra pūrva arddha bhāge ca brahma ādyāḥ aṣṭa śaktayaḥ brāhmī māheśvarī ca eva kaumārī vaiṣmavī tathā vārāhī ca eva māṃhendrī cāmuṇḍā ca eva saptamī mahā lakṣmīḥ aṣṭamī ca dvi bhujāḥ śoṇa vigrahāḥ kapālam utpalam ca eva bibhrāṇāḥ rakta vāsasaḥ atha vā anya prakāreṇa kecid dhyānam brahma ādi sadṛśa ākārāḥ brahma ādi sadṛśa āyudhāḥ brahma ādīnām param cihnam dhārayantyaḥ prakīrtitāḥ tāsām ūrdhva sthāna gatām mudrāḥ devyaḥ mahattarāḥ dāḍima puṣpa saṃkāśāḥ pīta ambara manoharāḥ catur bhujāḥ bhuja dvandva dhṛta carma kṛpāṇakāḥ mada rakta vilola akṣyaḥ tāsām nāmāni mat śṛṇu sarva saṃkṣobhiṇī ca eva sarva vidrāviṇī tathā sarva ākarṣaṇa kṛt mudrā tathā sarva vaśaṃkarā sarva unmādana mudrā ca yaṣṭiḥ sarva mahā aṅkuśā sarvakhecarikā mudrā sarvabījā tathā aparā sarvayoniḥ ca navamī tathā sarvatriśaṇḍikā siddhi brāhaya ādi mudrāḥ tāḥ etāḥ prakaṭa śaktayaḥ bhaṇḍa asurasya saṃhāram kartum rakta rathe sthitāḥ yāḥ guptā ākhyāḥ pūrvam uktāḥ tāsām nāmāni mat śṛṇu kāma ākarṣaṇikā ca eva buddhi ākarṣaṇikā kalā ahaṅkāra ākarṣiṇī ca śabda ākarṣaṇikā kalā sparśa ākarṣaṇikā nityā rūpa ākarṣaṇikā kalā rasa ākarṣaṇikā nityā gandha ākarṣaṇikā kalā citta ākarṣaṇikā nityā dhairya ākarṣaṇikā kalā mṛtyā karṣaṇikā nityā nāma ākarṇaṇikā kalā bīja ākarṣaṇikā nityā ca ātma karṣaṇikā kalā amṛta ākarṣaṇī nityā śarīra ākarṣiṇī kalā etāḥ ṣoḍaśa śītāṃśu kalā rūpāḥ ca śaktayaḥ aṣṭamam parva samprāptāḥ guptāḥ nāmnā prakīrtitāḥ vidruma druma saṃkāśāḥ mandasmita manoharāḥ cāpa bāṇau carma khaḍgau dadhānāḥ divya kāntayaḥ bhaṇḍa asura vadha arthāya pravṛttāḥ kumbhasambhava saptame parvaṇi kṛta āvāsāḥ guptatara abhidhāḥ anaṅga madana anaṅga madana āturayā saha ca anaṅgavegā anaṅgāṅkuśā api ca anaṅgam āligya aparāḥ etāḥ devyaḥ japā tviṣaḥ puṣpaśarān puṣpakandukam utpalam bhaṇḍāsuram abhikruddhāḥ prajvalatyaḥ iva sthitāḥ atha cakraratha indrasya ṣaṣṭham parva samāśritāḥ sarva saṃkṣobhiṇī mukhyāḥ sampradāya ākhyayā yutāḥ veṇī kṛta kaca stomāḥ sindūra tilaka ujjvalāḥ ati tīvra svabhāvāḥ ca kāla anala sama tviṣaḥ vahni bāṇam vahni cāpam vahni rūpam asim tathā vahni cakra ākhyā phalakam dadhānāḥ dīpta vigrahāḥ mahā śaktayaḥ eva etāḥ lalitāyāḥ mahā ojasaḥ sarva saṃkṣobhiṇī ca eva sarva vidrāviṇī tathā sarva ākarṣaṇikā śaktiḥ sarva āhlādinikā tathā sarva jṛṃbhaṇa śaktiḥ ca sarva unmādana śaktikā sarva artha sādhakā śaktiḥ sarva sampatti pūraṇī evam tu sampradāyānām nāmāni kathitāni vai atha pañcama parva sthāḥ kula uttīrṇāḥ iti smṛtāḥ tāḥ ca saptaṭika saṅkāśāḥ paraśum pāśam eva ca gadām ghaṇṭām maṇim ca eva dadhānāḥ dīpta vigrahāḥ deva dviṣam ati kruddhāḥ bhrukuṭi kuṭila ānanāḥ sarva priyaṅkarā devī sarva maṅgala kāriṇī sarva mṛtyu praśaminī sarva vighna nivāriṇī sarva aṅga sundarā devī sarva saubhāgya dāyinī daśa entāḥ kathitāḥ devyaḥ dayayā pūrita āśayāḥ cakre turīya parva sthāḥ muktā hāra sama tviṣaḥ nigarbha yoginī nāmnā prathitāḥ daśa kīrtitāḥ sarvajñā sarva śaktiḥ ca sarva aiśvarya pradā tathā sarva jñāna mayī devī sarva vyādhi vināśinī sarva ādhāra svarūpā ca sarva pāpa harā tathā sarva ānanda mayī devī sarva rakṣā svarūpiṇī daśamī devatā ajñeyā sarva iṣ phala pradā etāḥ catur bhujāḥ jñeyāḥ vajram śaktim ca tomaram cakram ca eva abhibibhrāṇāḥ bhaṇḍa asura vadha udyatāḥ atha cakraratha indrasya tṛtīyam parva saṃśritāḥ rahasyayoginī nāmnā prakhyātāḥ vāc adhīśvarāḥ rakta aśoka prasūna ābhā bāṇa kārmuka pāṇayaḥ kavaca channa sarva aṅgayaḥ vīṇā pustaka śobhitāḥ eva aruṇā ca javinī ākhyā sarva īśā kaulinī tathā aṣṭau etāḥ smṛtāḥ devyaḥ daitya saṃhāra hetavaḥ cāpa bāṇau pāna pātram mātuḥ uṅgam kṛpāṇikām tisraḥ tripīṭha nilayāḥ aṣṭa bāhu samanvitāḥ palakam nāgapāśam ca ghaṇṭām ca eva mahā dhvanim madirā mattāḥ ati gupta rahasyakāḥ kāmeśī ca eva vajreśī bhagamālinī atha aparā tisraḥ etāḥ smṛtāḥ devyaḥ bhaṇḍe kopa samanvitāḥ lalitā sama māhātmyāḥ lalitā sama tejasaḥ etāḥ tu nityam śrī devyāḥ antaraṅgāḥ prakīrtitāḥ paritas racita āvāsāḥ proktāḥ pañcadaśa akṣarāḥ tithi nityāḥ kāla rūpāḥ viśvam vyāpya eva saṃsthitāḥ bhaṇḍa asura ādi daityeṣu prakṣubdha bhrukuṭi taṭāḥ devī sama nija ākārāḥ devī sama nija āyudhāḥ jagatām upakārāya vartamānāḥ yuge yuge tāsām nāmāni mattaḥ tvam avadhāraya kumbhaja kāmeśī bhagamālā ca nityaklinnā tathā eva ca bheruṇḍā vahnivāsinyaḥ mahāvajreśvarī tathā nityā nīlapatākā ca vijayā sarvamaṅgalā daśa pañca ca kīrtitāḥ etābhiḥ sahitā devī sadā sevā ekabuddhibhiḥ duṣṭam bhaṇḍāsuram jetum niryayau parameśvarī sapta parvāṇi ca uktāni tatra devyāḥ ca tāḥ śṛṇu saṃgītayoginī proktā śrī devyāḥ ativallabhā ratiḥ prītiḥ manojā ca vīṇā kārmuka pāṇayaḥ tamāla śyāmala ākārāḥ dānava unmūlana kṣamāḥ tṛtīya parva saṃrūḍhā manobhū bāṇa devatā drāviṇī śoṣiṇī ca eva bandhinī mohinī tathā unmādinī iti pañca etāḥ dīpta kārmuka pāṇayaḥ kastūrī tilaka ullāsi bhālā muktā virājitāḥ kavaca channa sarva aṅgāḥ palāśa prasava tviṣaḥ pañca kāmāḥ ime proktāḥ bhaṇḍa asura vadha arthinaḥ brahmī mukhyāḥ tu pūrva uktāḥ caṇḍikā tu aṣṭamā parā ratiḥ prītiḥ kīrti śāntī puṣṭiḥ tuṣṭiḥ ca śaktayaḥ etāḥ ca krodha rakta akṣāḥ daityam hantum mahā balam kunta cakra dharāḥ proktāḥ kumāryaḥ kumbha sambhava pañcamam parva saṃprāptāḥ vāmā ādyāḥ ṣoḍaśā aparāḥ gītim cakruḥ ratha indrasya tāsām nāmāni mat śṛṇu vāmā jyeṣṭā ca raudrī ca śāntiḥ śraddhā sarasvatī śrī bhū śāktiḥ ca lakṣmīḥ ca sṛṣṭiḥ ca eva tu mohinī tathā pramāthinī ca aśvasinī vīciḥ tathā eva ca etāḥ tu kuravinda ābhāḥ jagat kṣobhaṇa lampaṭāḥ mahā sarasam annāham ādadhānāḥ pade pade vajra kaṅkaṭa saṃchannāḥ aṭṭahāsa ujjvalāḥ pare vajra daṇḍau śataghnīm ca saṃbibhrāṇāḥ bhuśuṇḍikāḥ atha gīti ratha indrasya ṣaṣṭham parva samāśritāḥ asitāṅga prabhṛtayaḥ bhairavāḥ śastra bhīṣaṇāḥ tri śikham pāna pātram ca bibhrāṇāḥ nīla varcasaḥ asitāṅgaḥ ruruḥ caṇḍaḥ krodhaḥ unmattabhairavaḥ kapālī bhīṣaṇaḥ ca eva saṃhāraḥ ca aṣṭa bhairavāḥ mātaṅgī siddhalakṣmīḥ ca mahāmātaṅgikā api ca mahatī siddha lakṣmīḥ ca śoṇāḥ bāṇa dhanus dharāḥ durgā ambā baṭukaḥ ca iṃva sarve te śastra pāṇayaḥ śaṅkhaḥ padmaḥ nidhiḥ ca eva te sarve śastra pāṇayaḥ loka dviṣam prati kruddhāḥ bhaṇḍam caṇḍa parākramam śakra ādayaḥ ca viṣmu antāḥ daśa diś cakra nāyakāḥ śakti rūpāḥ tatra parvaṇi adhastāt kṛta saṃśrayāḥ vajre śaktim kāladaṇḍam akim pāśam dhvajam tathā gadām triśūlam darbha astram vajram ca dadhataḥ tu amī sevante mantri nāthām tām nityam bhakti samanvitāḥ bhaṇḍa asurān durdurūḍhān nihantum viśva kaṇṭakān mantri nātha āśraya dvārā lalitā jñāpana utsukāḥ gīti cakra ratha upānte dikpālāḥ saṃśrayam daduḥ sarveṣām ca eva devānām mantriṇī dvāratas kṛtā vijñāpanā mahādevyāḥ kārya siddhim prayacchati rākṣī vijñāpanā ca iti pradhāna dvārāt kṛtā yathā khalu phala prāptiḥ sevakānām hi jāyate anyathā katham eteṣām sāmarthyam jvalita ojasaḥ apadhṛṣya prabhāvāyāḥ śrī devyāḥ upasarpaṇe sā hi saṃgīta vidyā iti śrī devyāḥ ativallabhā na atilaṅghati ca kvāpi tat uktam kārya siddhiṣu śrī devyāḥ śakti sāmrājye sarva karmāṇi mantriṇī tasmāt sarve api dikpālāḥ śrī devyāḥ jaya kāṅkṣiṇaḥ tasyāḥ pradhāna bhūtāyāḥ sevām eva vitanvate iti śrī lalitā devyāḥ cakrarāja ratha uttame parva sthitānām devīnām nāmāni kathitāni alam bhaṇḍa asurasya saṃhāre tasyāḥ divya āyudhāni api imāni sarva devīnām nāmāni ākarṇayanti ye iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalita upakhyāne śrīcakrarājarathajñeyacakrarathaparvasthadevatānāmaprakāśanam nāma ekonaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ devatāḥ ca śṛṇu prājña nāma yat śṛṇvatām jayaḥ prathamam parva bindu ākhyam saṃprāptā daṇḍanāyikā sā tatra jagat uddaṇḍa kaṇṭaka vrāta ghasmarī nānāvidhābhiḥ jvālābhiḥ nartayantī jaya śriyam daṃṣṭra bāla mṛgāṅka aṃśu vibhāvana vibhāvarī prāvṛṣeṇya payovāha vyūha nīla vapus llatā potriṇī putrita aśeṣa viśvāvarta kadambikā tasya eva rathanābhasya dvitīyam parva saṃśritāḥ jṛṃbhinī mohinī ca eva staṃbhinī tisraḥ eva hi utphulla dāḍima prakhyam sarva dānava mardanāḥ musalam ca halam hālā pātram maṇi gaṇa arpitam jvalat māṇikya valayaiḥ bi bhrāṇāḥ pāṇipallavaiḥ ati tīkṣṇa karāla akṣyaḥ jvālābhiḥ daitya sainikān dahatyaḥ iva niḥśaṅkam sevante sūkara ānanām kiri cakra ratha indrasya tṛtīyam parva saṃśritāḥ andhinī ādyāḥ pañca devyaḥ devīyantra kṛta āspadāḥ yad jvālāḥ iva tu kalpa agneḥ aṅganā veṣam āśritāḥ bhaṇḍāsurasya sarveṣām sainyānām rudhira plutim lilikṣamāṇāḥ jihvābhiḥ lelihānābhiḥ ujjvalāḥ sevante īm satatam daṇḍa nāthām uddaṇḍa vikramām brahma ādyāḥ pañcamī varjyāḥ aṣṭamīra varjitāḥ api ṣaḍ eva devyaḥ ṣaṣ cakra jvalat jvālā kalevarāḥ mayā ājñayā daṇḍanāthāyāḥ tam pradeśam upāsate tasya eva parvaṇaḥ adhastāt tvaritāḥ sthānam āśritāḥ yakṣiṇī śaṅkhinī ca eva lākinī hākinī tathā śākinī ḍākinī ca eva tāsām aikya svarūpiṇī iti tvacam raktam tathā māṃsam medaḥ asthi ca virodhinām majjānam atha śukram ca pibantayaḥ vikaṭa ānanāḥ niṣṭhuraiḥ siṃhanādaiḥ ca pūrayatyaḥ diśaḥ daśa dhātu nāthāḥ iti proktāḥ aṇima ādi aṣṭa siddhi dāḥ mohane māraṇe ca eva stambhane tāḍane tathā bhakṣaṇe duṣṭa daityānām āmūlam ca nikṛntane paṇḍitāḥ khaṇḍita aśeṣa vipadaḥ bhakti śāliṣu dhātu nāthāḥ iti proktāḥ sarva dhātuṣu saṃsthitāḥ sapta api vāridhīn ūrmi mālā saṃcuṃbita ambarān kṣaṇa ṛdhena eva niṣpātum niṣpanna bahu sāhasāḥ māra dantāḥ ca bhayaṅkara vilocanāḥ sva svāminī droha kṛtām svakīya samaya druhām vaidika drohaṇāt eva drohiṇām vīra vairiṇām yajña droha kṛtām duṣṭa daityānām bhakṣaṇe samāḥ nityam eva ca sevante potriṇīm daṇḍanāyikām deva dviṣām camū rakta hālā pāna mahā uddhate sadā vighūrṇamāna akṣyau sadā prahasita ānane ābibhrāṇam vibudhaiḥ smṛtam etad āyudha yugmena lalitā daḍanāyikā khaṇḍayiṣyati saṃgrāmam viṣaṅgam nāma dānaham tasya eva parvaṇaḥ daṇḍanāthāyāḥ agra sīmani daṃṣṭra kaṭakaṭātkāra badhirīkṛta diṅmukhaḥ caṇḍoccaṇḍaḥ iti khyātaḥ catur hastaḥ trilocanaḥ śūla khaḍga pretapāśān dadhānaḥ dīpta vigrahaḥ sadā saṃsevate devīm paśyan eva hi potriṇīm kiri cakra ratha indrasya ṣaṣṭam parva samāśritāḥ mārttālī ādyāḥ aṣṭa devyaḥ dikṣu aṣṭāsu upaviśrutāḥ aṣṭa parvata niṣpāta ghora nirghāta niḥsvanāḥ aṣṭa nāga sphurat bhūṣāḥ anaṣṭa bala tejasaḥ prakṛṣṭa dos prakāṇḍa ūṣma huta dānava koṭayaḥ sevante lalitām devyaḥ daṇḍanāthām aharniśam tāsām ākhyāḥ ca vikhyātāḥ samākarṇaya kumbhaja vārtālī ca eva vārāhīsā vārāhamukhī parā andhinī rodhinī ca eva jṛṃbhiṇī ca eva mohinī stambhinī iti ripu kṣobha stambhana uccāṭana kṣamāḥ tāsām ca parvaṇaḥ vāma bhāge satata saṃsthitiḥ daṇḍanātha upavāhyaḥ tu kāsaraḥ dhūsara ākṛtiḥ ardha krośa āyataḥ śṛṅga dvitaye krośa vigrahaḥ khaḍga vat niṣṭhuraiḥ loma jātaiḥ saṃvṛta vigrahaḥ kāla daṇḍa vat uccaṇḍa bāla kāṇḍa bhayaṅkaraḥ nīlāñjana acala prakhyaḥ vikaṭa unnata ruṣṭa bhūḥ mahānīla giri śreṣṭha gariṣṭha skandha maṇḍalaḥ prabhūta ūṣmala niśvāsa prasara ākaṃpita ambudhiḥ tasya eva parvaṇaḥ adhastāt citra sthāna kṛta ālayāḥ indra ādayaḥ aneka bhedāḥ diśām aṣṭaka devatāḥ lalitāyām kārya siddhim vijñāpayitum āgatāḥ indraḥ ca apsarasaḥ ca eva sa catuḥṣaṣṭi koṭayaḥ siddha agniḥ ca sādhyāḥ ca viśvedevāḥ tathā apare viśvakarmā mayaḥ ca eva mātaraḥ ca bala unnatāḥ rudrāḥ ca paricārāḥ ca rudrāḥ ca eva piśācakāḥ krandan cirakṣasām nāthāḥ rākṣasāḥ bahavaḥ tathā mitrāḥ ca tatra gandharvāḥ sadā gāna viśāradāḥ viśvāvasu prabhṛtayaḥ vikhyātāḥ tad purogamāḥ tathā bhūta gaṇāḥ ca anye varuṇaḥ vāsavaḥ pare vidyādharāḥ kinnarāḥ ca māruteśvaraḥ eva ca tathā citrarathaḥ ca eva rathakāraka kārakāḥ tumburuḥ nāradaḥ yakṣaḥ somaḥ yakṣeśvaraḥ tathā īśānaḥ ca jagat cakra bhakṣakaḥ śūla bhīṣaṇaḥ brahmā ca eva aśvinī putraḥ vaidya vidyā viśāradau dhanvantariḥ ca bhagavān atha anye gaṇanāyakāḥ kaṭa kāṇḍa galat dāna saṃtarpita madhu vratāḥ mahāpadmaḥ śaṅkhapālaḥ gulikaḥ subalaḥ tathā ete nāga īśvarāḥ ca eva nāga koṭibhiḥ āvṛtāḥ pūrva ādi diśam ārabhya paritas kṛta mandirāḥ tatra eva devatāḥ cakre cakra ākārāḥ marut diśaḥ māśritya kila vartante tad adhiṣṭhātṛ devatāḥ jṛṃbhiṇī staṃbhinī ca eva mohinī tisraḥ eva ca kapālam ca gadām bibhrat ūrdhva keśaḥ mahā vapūḥ pātāla tala jambāla bahulā kāra kālimā aṭṭahāsa mahā vajra dīrṇa brahmāṇḍa maṇḍalaḥ phūtkārī tripurā yuktam phaṇi pāśam kare vahan kṣetrapālaḥ sadā bhāti sevamānaḥ kiṭīśvarīm pravavṛte prāk uktam eva deveśī vāha siṃhasya lakṣaṇam tasya eva parvaṇaḥ adhastāt daṇḍanāthā sama tviṣaḥ daṇḍinī sadṛśa aśeṣa bhūṣaṇa āyudha maṇḍitāḥ śamyāḥ kroḍa ānanāḥ candra rekhā uttaṃsita kuntalāḥ lalitā drohinīm śyāmā drohinīm svāminī druhām nija bhakta droha kṛtāḥ mantra mālā vibhūṣaṇāḥ sva goṣṭhī samāyā kṣepa kāriṇām muṇḍa maṇḍalaiḥ sahasram devatāḥ proktāḥ sevamānāḥ kiṭīśvarīm tāsām nāmāni sarvāsām daṇḍinyāḥ kumbha saṃbhava sahasranāma adhyāye tu vakṣyante na adhunā punar atha tāsām devatānām kolāsyānām samīpatas māhanam kṛṣṇa sāraṅgaḥ daṇḍinyāḥ samaye sthitaḥ krośa ardha ardha āyataḥ śṛṅge tad ardha ardha āyataḥ mukhe sadā ca uddhṛta vāladhiḥ udare dhavala chāyaḥ huṅkāreṇa mahīyasā madirā sindhuḥ devatā rūpam āsthitā māṇikya giri vat śoṇam haste piśita piṇḍakam dadhānā na akṣī hema aṃbhoja sraj āvṛtā mada śaktyā samāśliṣṭāḥ dhṛta rakta sarojayā yadā yadā bhaṇḍa daityaḥ saṃgrāme saṃpravartate yuddha sveda manuprāptāḥ śaktayaḥ syuḥ pipāsitāḥ tadā tadā surā sindhuḥ ātmānam bahudhā kṣipan raṇe khedam devatānām añjasā apākariṣyati tadā śroṣyasi saṃgrāme kathyamānam mayā mudā upari api kṛta āvāsāḥ hetuka ādyāḥ daśa smṛtāḥ mahantaḥ bhairava śreṣṭhāḥ khyātāḥ atha bhagnam samāśvāsya nijam balam ariṃdamaḥ dīrgha grīvaḥ samunnaddhaḥ pṛṣṭhe niṣṭhura todanaḥ dhiṣṭhitaḥ durmadena vāhana uṣṭraḥ cacāla ha tam uṣṭra vāhanam duṣṭam anvīyuḥ kruddha cetasaḥ dānau anaśvasat sarvān bhītān śakti yuyutsayā saṃpad karīcamū cakram vanam vārbhiḥ iva ambudaḥ tena duḥsaha sattvena tāḍitāḥ bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ staṃbhitā iva abhavat senā saṃpad karyāḥ kṣaṇam raṇe atha krodha aruṇam cakṣuḥ dadhānā saṃpad aṃbikā raṇa kolāhala gajam ārūḍhā ayudhyata amunā ālola kaṅkaṇa kvāṇa ramaṇīyataraḥ karaḥ tasyāḥ ca ākṛṣya kodaṇḍa maurvīm ākarṇam āhave laghu hasta tayā apaśyan ākṛṣṭat na ca mokṣaṇam dadṛśe ghanuṣaḥ cakram kevalam śara dhāraṇe āśu arka abara samparka sphuṭa pratiphalat phalāḥ śarāḥ sampad karī cāpa cyutāḥ samadahan arīn abhūt anyonya saṃghaṭṭāt visphuliṅga śilīmukhaiḥ prathamam prasṛtaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sampad devī suradviṣoḥ tad antare ca bāṇānām ati saṃghaṭṭa yonayaḥ tayā adhirūḍhaḥ saṃśroṇī āraṇa kolāhalaḥ karī parākramam bahuvidham darśayāmāsa saṃgare kareṇa katicid daityān pāda ghātena kāṃścana udagra danta musala ghātaiḥ anyān ca dānavān vāla kāṇḍa hataiḥ anyān phetkāraiḥ aparān ripūn pṛthu māna abhighātena kāṃścid daityān vyamardayat caturam caritam cakre saṃpad devī mataṃga jaḥ su durmadaḥ krudhā raktaḥ dṛḍhena ekena patriṇā saṃpad karī mukuṭa gam maṇim ekam apāharat atha krodha aruṇa dṛśā tayā muktaiḥ śilīmukhaiḥ vikṣataḥ vakṣasi kṣipram durmadaḥ jīvitam jahau tatas kilakilā rāvam kṛtvā śakti camū varaiḥ hata avaśiṣṭāḥ daityāḥ tu śakti bāṇaiḥ khilīkṛtāḥ palāyitāḥ raṇa kṣoṇyāḥ śūnyakam puram āśrayan tad vṛttāntam atha ākarṇya saṃkruddhaḥ dānava īśvaraḥ pracaṇḍena prabhāvena dīpyamānaḥ iva ātmani kuṭila akṣam nikaṭa gam babhāṣe pṛtanāpatim katham sā duṣṭa vanitā durmadam bala śālinam nipātitavatī yuddhe kaṣṭaḥ eva vidheḥ kramaḥ tām duṣṭa vanitām jetum ākraṣṭum ca kacam haṭhāt senāpatim kuraṇḍa ākhyam preṣaya āhava durmadam eti saṃproṣitaḥ tena kuṭilākṣaḥ mahā palam puraṇḍam caṇḍa dos daṇḍam ājuhāva prabhoḥ puras sa kuraṇḍaḥ samāgatya praṇāma svāmine adiśat uvāca kuṭila akṣaḥ tam gaccha sajjaya sainikān māyāyām caturaḥ asi tvam citra yuddha viśārada kūṭa yuddhe ca nipuṇaḥ tām striyam parimardaya iti svāmi puras tena kuṭilākṣeṇa deśitaḥ nirjagāma purāt tūrṇam kuraṇḍaḥ caṇḍa vikramaḥ viṃśati akṣauhiṇībhiḥ ca samantāt parivāritaḥ durmadasya agrajaḥ caṇḍaḥ kuraṇḍaḥ samaram yayau dūlībhiḥ tumulīkurvan diś antam dhīra mānasaḥ śārṅgam dhanuḥ samādāya ghora ṭaṅkāram utsvanam vavarṣa śara dhārabhiḥ saṃpad karyā mahā camūm vṛthak vahasi vikrānti lava leśam mahā madam idānīm ca eva bhavatīm etaiḥ nārāca maṇḍalaiḥ antakasya purīm atra prāpayiṣyāmi paśya mām apūrvam aṅganā raktam pibantu raṇapūtanāḥ sainyam protsāhayāmāsa śakti senā vimardane atha tām pṛtanām caṇḍī kuraṇḍasya mahā ojasaḥ apurva āhava saṃjāta kautukā atha jagāda tām aśva rūḍhā samāgatya sa sneha ārdram idam vacaḥ sakhi saṃpatkari prītyā mama vāṇī yācitā asi sakhī tvena na atra saṃśayam ācara iti tasyāḥ vacaḥ śrutvā saṃpad devyā śuci smitā nivartayāmāsa camūm kuruṇḍa abhimukha utthitām atha bāla arka varṇābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ samadhiṣṭhitāḥ taraṃgāḥ iva sainya abdheḥ turaṃgāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ kharaiḥ khura puṭaiḥ kṣoṇīm ullikhantaḥ muhur muhur cāreṣu pañcadhā khura pātane protsāhane ca saṃjñābhiḥ kara pāda agra yonibhiḥ caturābhiḥ turaṃgasya hṛdaya jñābhiḥ āhave aśva ārūḍha ambikā sainya śaktibhiḥ saha dānavāḥ protsāhitāḥ kuraṇḍena samayudhyanta durmadāḥ evam pravṛtte samare śaktīnām ca suradviṣām abhyadravat durācāram aśva ārūḍhāḥ kuraṇḍakam saṃdhyā anurakta śītāṃśu maṇḍala sundara ānanā smayamānā iva samare gṛhīta maṇi kārmukā avākirat śara āsāraiḥ kuraṇḍam turaga ānanā turaga ārūḍhayā utkṣiptāḥ samākrāman digantarān diśaḥ daśa vyānaśire rukma puṅkhāḥ śilīmukhāḥ durmadasya agrajaḥ kruddhaḥ kuraṇḍaḥ caṇḍa vikramaḥ viśikhaiḥ śārṅga niṣṭhyūtaiḥ aśva ārūḍhā mavākirat caṇḍaiḥ khura puṭaiḥ sainyam khaṇḍayan ati vegataḥ aśva ārūḍha aturaṅgaḥ api mardayāmāsa dānavān tasyāḥ heṣā ravāt dūram utpāta ambudhi niḥsvanaḥ amūrcchayan anekāni tasya ānītāni vairiṇaḥ nijam pāśa āyudham divyam mumoca jvalita ākṛti tasmāt pāśāt koṭiśas anye pāśāḥ bhujaga bhīṣaṇāḥ chinnam aurvi dhanuḥ tyaktvā bhṛśam kruddhā haya āsanā aṅkuśam pātayāmāsa tasya vakṣasi durmateḥ tena aṅkuśena jvalatā pīta jīvita śoṇitaḥ tad aṅkuśa viniṣṭhyūtāḥ putanāḥ kāścid udbhaṭāḥ tat sainyam pāśa nisyandam bhakṣayitvā kṣayam gatāḥ ittham kuruṇḍe nihate viṃśati akṣauhiṇī patau hata avaśiṣṭāḥ te daityāḥ prapalāyanta vai drutam kuraṇḍam sa anujam yuddhe śakti sainyaiḥ nipātitam śrutvā śūnyaka nāthaḥ api niśaśvāsa bhujaṃga vat iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne durmadakuraṇḍavadhaḥ nāma dvāviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha aśva rūḍhayā kṣipte kuraṇḍe bhaṇḍa dānavaḥ yat ca no śaṅkitam citte tat etat kaṣṭam āgatam duṣṭa dāsyāḥ prabhāvaḥ ayam māyāvinyāḥ mahattaraḥ itas param karaṅka ādīn pañca senā adhināyakān śatam akṣauhiṇīnām ca prasthāpaya raṇa aṅgaṇe te yuddha durmadāḥ śūrāḥ saṃgrāmeṣu tanutyajaḥ iti bhaṇḍa vacaḥ śrutvā bhṛśam catvarayā anvitaḥ kuṭilākṣaḥ karaṅka ādīn ājuhāva camūpatīn te svāminam namaskṛtya kuṭilākṣeṇa deśitāḥ teṣām prayāṇa niḥsāṇa raṇitam bhṛśa duḥsaham mākarṇya diggajāḥ tūrṇam śīrṇa karṇāḥ jughūrṇire śatam akṣauhiṇīnām ca prācalat ketumālakam hreṣamāṇa haya ākīrṇam krandat bhaṭa kula udbhavam bṛṃhamāṇa gajam garjat ratha yakram cacāla tat cakranemi hata kṣoṇī reṇu kṣapita rociṣā dhūli mayam iva aśeṣam abhavat viśva maṇḍalam udbhūtaiḥ dhūlikā jālaiḥ ākrāntāḥ daitya sainikāḥ iyat tayā atas senāyāḥ saṃkhyā api paribhāvitā dhvajāḥ bahuvidha ākārāḥ mīna vyāla ādi citritāḥ ha vitresuḥ amarāḥ sarve śaktīnām bhaṅga śaṅkayā te karaṅka mukhāḥ pañca senāpatayaḥ uddhatāḥ sarpiṇīm nāma samare māyām cakruḥ mahīyasam taiḥ samutpatitā duṣṭā sarpiṇī ramaśāmbarī dhūmravarṇā ca dhūmroṣṭhī dhūmravarmapayodharā puras cacāla śaktīn āntrāsayatī manaḥ raṇe kadrūḥ iva aparā duṣṭā bahu sarpa vibhūṣaṇā sarpāṇām udbhava sthānam māyā maya śarīriṇām senāpatīnām nāsīre vellayantī mahī tale mahudhā cakre ghora ārāva virāviṇī tathā eva māyayā pūrvam te asura idrāḥ vyajījayan karaṅka ādyāḥ durātmānaḥ pañca pañcattva kāmukāḥ atha pravavṛte yuddham śaktīnām amara druhām anyonya vīra bhāṣābhiḥ protsāhita ghana atyanta saṃkula tayā na vijñāta parasparāḥ śaktayaḥ dānavaḥ ca eva prajahuḥ śastra pāṇayaḥ anyonya śastra saṃghaṭṭa samutthita hutāśane ati niṣṭhura vidhvaṃsi siṃhanāda bhayaṃkare rajaḥ mule rākṣasī tṛpti dāyini mad strī śaraṇi vicchinna daitya kaṇṭha utthita pravṛtte ghora saṃgrāme śaktīnām ca suradviṣām atha sva balam ādāya pañcabhiḥ preritā satī sarpiṇī bahudhā sarpān visasarja śarīrāt takṣa karkeṭaka samāḥ vāsuki pramukha tviṣaḥ nānāvidha vapus varṇāḥ nānā dṛṣṭi bhayaṃkarāḥ nānāvidha viṣa jvālā nirdagdha bhuvana trayāḥ dāradam vatsanābham ca kālakūṭam atha aparam saurāṣṭram ca viṣam ghoram brahmaputram atha aparam pratipannam śauklikeyam anyāni api viṣāṇi ca dhūmra varṇāḥ dvi vadanā sarpāḥ ati bhayaṅkarāḥ nayana dvaṃdvāḥ dutthitāḥ krodha dīpitāḥ pīta varṇāḥ triphaṇakāḥ daṃṣṭrābhiḥ vikaṭa ānanāḥ sarpiṇyāḥ karṇa kuharāt utthitāḥ sarpa koṭayaḥ āsya ādāḥ nīla vapuṣaḥ sarpiṇyāḥ phaṇinaḥ abhavan anyaiḥ ca bala varṇāḥ ca catur vaktrāḥ catuṣpadāḥ nāsikā vivarāt tasyāḥ udgatāḥ ugra rociṣaḥ lambamāna mahā carma āvṛtta sthūla payodharāt nābhikuṇḍāt ca bahavaḥ rakta varṇāḥ bhayānakāḥ halāhalam vahantaḥ ca protthitāḥ pannaga adhipāḥ bidaśantaḥ śakti senām dahantaḥ viṣa vahnibhiḥ badhnantaḥ bhoga pāśaiḥ ca nighnantaḥ phaṇa maṇḍalaiḥ atyantam ākulām cakruḥ lalitā īśā camūm amī khaṇḍyamānāḥ api muhur śaktīnām śastra koṭibhiḥ naśyanti bahavaḥ sarpāḥ jāyante ca apare punar mūla bhūtā yatas duṣṭā sarpiṇī na vinaśyati atas tad kṛta sarpāṇām nāśe sarpa antara udbhavaḥ tatas ca śakti sainyānām śarīrāṇi viṣa analaiḥ kiṅkartavya vimūḍheṣu śakti cakreṣu bhogibhiḥ parākramam bahuvidham cakruḥ te pañca dānavāḥ cakreṇa tīkṣṇa dhāreṇa śakti senām amardayat vajradanta abhidhaḥ ca anyaḥ bhaṇḍa daitya camūpatiḥ vajra bāṇa abhighātena ha uṣṭrāt hi raṇam vyadhāt vajradanta abhidhānaḥ anyaḥ camūnām adhipaḥ balī gṛdhra yugma ratha ārūḍhaḥ prajahāra śilīmukhaiḥ taiḥ senāpatibhiḥ duṣṭaiḥ protsāhitam atha āhave śatam akṣauhiṇīnām ca nipapāta eka helayā ca durācārā bahu māyā parigrahā kṣaṇekṣaṇe koṭi saṃkhyān visasarja phaṇa adharān nakulī garuḍa ārūḍhā sā papāta raṇa ajire samasta vāc maya ākārā dantaiḥ vajra mayaiḥ yutā tayā adhiṣṭhita tuṅga aṃsaḥ pakṣa vikṣipta bhūdharaḥ sarpiṇī māyayā jātān sarpān dṛṣṭvā bhayānakān atha śrī nakulī devyāḥ dvātriṃśat danta koṭayaḥ dvātriṃśat koṭayaḥ jātāḥ nakulāḥ kanaka prabhāḥ itas tatas khaṇḍayantaḥ sarpiṇī sarpa maṇḍalam nija daṃṣṭra vimardena nāśayantaḥ ca tat viṣam utkarṇāḥ krodha samparkāt hūnita aśeṣa lomakāḥ utphullāḥ nakulāḥ vyātta vadanāḥ vyadaśan ahīn tīkṣṇa danta nipātena khaṇḍayāmāsa vigraham bhogi bhoga sṛtaiḥ raktaiḥ sṛkkiṇī śoṇa tām gate nakulaiḥ daśyamānānām atyanta caṭulam vapuḥ muhur kuṇḍalitaiḥ bhogaiḥ pannagānām vyaceṣṭata nakula āvali daṣṭānām naṣṭa asūnām phaṇābhṛtām phaṇa ābhara samutkīrṇāḥ maṇayaḥ vyarucan raṇe nakula āghāta saṃśīrṇa phaṇā cakraiḥ vinirgataiḥ phaṇayaḥ tad mahā droha vahvi jvālāḥ iva ābabhuḥ evaṃprakārataḥ babhru maṇḍalaiḥ avakhaṇḍite māyā maye sarpa jāle sarpiṇī kopam ādadhe tayā saha mahat yuddham kṛtvā sā nakula īśvarā gāruḍa astram ati krūram samādhatta śilīmukhe tat gāruḍa astram uddāma jvālā dīpita diṅmukham praviśya sarpiṇī deham sarpa māyām vyaśoṣayat māyā śaktoḥ vināśena sarpiṇī vilayam gatā ca tad vināśena prāptāḥ pañca camū varāḥ sā sarpiṇī kathā śeṣam nītā nakula vīryāt atas sva bala nāśena bhṛśam kruddhāḥ camū carāḥ ekā eva sā tārkṣyarathā pañcabhiḥ pṛtanā īśvarā paṭṭiśaiḥ musalaiḥ ca eva bhindipālaiḥ sahasraśas tatas hāhā rutam ghoram kurvāṇāḥ daitya kiṅkarāḥ udagra daṃśa nakulaiḥ nakulaiḥ ākulīkṛtāḥ utpatya gaganāt kecid ghora cītkāra kāriṇaḥ karṇeṣu daṣṭvā nāsāyām anye daṣṭāḥ śiraḥ taṭe pṛṣṭhatas pyadaśan kecid ā gatya vyākṛta kriyāḥ vikalāḥ chinna varmāṇaḥ bhaya visrasta śastrikāḥ kecid praviśya nakulāḥ vyāttāni āsyāni vairiṇām bhogi bhogāni vā ākṛṣya vyadaśan rasanā talam anye karṇeṣu nakulāḥ prāviśan deva vairiṇām sūkṣma rūpāḥ viśantisma nānā randhrāṇi babhravaḥ nija sainyāni dīnāni karaṅkaḥ kopam āsthitaḥ anye api ca camū nāthāḥ laghu hastāḥ mahā balāḥ pratibabhru śara stomān vavṛṣuḥ vāridāḥ iva daitya sainya pati prauḍha kodaḍa utthāḥ śilīmukhāḥ babhrūṇām danta koṭīṣu kaṭhora ghaṭṭanam vyadhuḥ camūpati śakhi ūhaiḥ āhatebhyaḥ paraḥśataiḥ babhrūṇām vajra datebhyaḥ niścakrāma hutāśanaḥ pañca api te camū nātha visṛṣṭaiḥ eka helayā itas tatas camū nātha vikṣipta śara koṭibhiḥ viśīrṇa gātrāḥ nakulāḥ nakulīm paryavārayan atha sā nakulī vāṇī vāṅmayasya eka nāyikā nakulānām parāvṛttyā mahantam roṣam āśritā akṣīṇanakulam nāma mahā astram sarvatomukham vahni jvālā parīta agram saṃdadhe śārṅgadhanvani tad astrataḥ viniṣṭhyūtāḥ nakulāḥ koṭi saṃkhyākāḥ javāḥ vajra sārāḥ ca nibiḍā vajra jāla bhayaṅkarā vajra ākāraiḥ naśaiḥ tūrṇa dārayantaḥ mahī talam vajra ratna prakāśena locanena api śobhitāḥ vajra sampāta sadṛśāḥ nāsā cītkāra kāriṇaḥ mardayanti sura arāti sainyam daśana koṭibhiḥ vinaṣṭāḥ pratyavayavam vineśuḥ dānava adhamāḥ evam vajra mayaiḥ babhuḥ maṇḍalaiḥ śaṇḍite bale śatākṣauhiṇike saṃkhye te sva mātra avaśeṣitāḥ ati trāsena roṣeṇa gṛhītāḥ ca camū varāḥ saṃgrāmam adhikam tenuḥ samākṛṣṭa śarāsanāḥ taiḥ samam bahudhā yuddham tanvānā nakula īśvarā paṭṭiśena karaṅkasya ciccheda kaṭhinam śiraḥ kāka vāśita sukhyānām caturṇām api vairiṇām utpatya utpatya tārkṣyeṇa vyalunāt asinā śiraḥ tādṛśam lāghavam dṛṣṭvā nakulyā śyāmala ambikā bahu mene mahā sattvām duṣṭa asura vināśinīm nija aṅga deva tattvam ca tasyai śyāmā ambikā dadau lokottare guṇe dṛṣṭe kasya na prīti saṃbhavaḥ hata śiṣṭāḥ bhīta bhītāḥ nakulī śaraṇam gatāḥ sā api tān vīkṣya kṛpayā mā bhaiṣṭa iti vihasya ca bhavat rājñe raṇa udantam aśeṣam ca nibodhata tayā evam preṣitāḥ śīghram tat ālokya raṇa kṣitim muditāḥ te punar bhītyā śūnya kāyām palāyitāḥ tad udantam tatas śrutvā bhaṇḍaḥ caṇḍaḥ ruṣā abhavat iti brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge lalitopākhyāne karaṅkādipañcasenāpativadhaḥ nāma trayoviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ hateṣu teṣu roṣa andhaḥ niśvasan śūnyakeśvaraḥ proce yuyutsā vyākula āśayaḥ karaṅka ādyaḥ camū nāthāḥ kandalat bhuja vikramāḥ sarpiṇī māyayā sarva gīrvāṇa mada bhañjanāḥ pāpīyasā tayā gūḍha māyayā vinipātitāḥ balāhaka prabhṛtayaḥ sapta ye sainika adhipāḥ tri śatam ca akṣauhiṇīnām prasthāpaya saha eva taiḥ te mardayitvā lalitā sainyam māyā parāyaṇāḥ kīkasa garbha saṃjātāḥ te pracaṇḍa parākramāḥ balāhaka mukhāḥ sapta bhrātaraḥ jayinaḥ sadā teṣām avaśyam vijayaḥ bhaviṣyati raṇa aṅgaṇe iti bhaṇḍāsureṇa uktaḥ kuṭilākṣaḥ samāhvayat balāhaka mukhān sapta senā nāthān mada utkaṭān balāhakaḥ prathamatas tasmāt sūcīmukhaḥ aparaḥ anyaḥ phāla mukhaḥ ca eva vikarṇaḥ vikaṭa ānanaḥ karālāyūḥ karaṭakaḥ saptā ete vīrya śālinaḥ bhaṇḍāsuram namaskṛtya yuddha kautūhala ulvaṇāḥ sarve bhrātaraḥ anyonyam āvṛtāḥ tri śāta akṣauhiṇī senā senān yaḥ anvagaman tadā ghora saṃgrāmiṇī pādā ghātaiḥ mardita bhū talā pibanti dhūlikā jālaiḥ aśeṣān api sāgarān bherī niḥ sāṇa taṃpoṭṭa paṇava ānaka nisvanaiḥ nabhaḥ guṇa mayam viśvam ādadhānāḥ pade pade tri śata akṣauhiṇī senām tām gṛhītvā madet hatāḥ dhṛta roṣa aruṇāḥ sūrya maṇḍalaḥ ddīpta kaṅkaṭāḥ uddīpta śastra bharaṇāḥ celuḥ dīpta ūrdhva keśinaḥ sapta lokān pramathitum proṣitāḥ pūrvam uddhatāḥ bhaṇḍa asureṇa mahatā jagat vijaya kāriṇā sapta loka vimardena tena dṛṣṭvā mahā balāḥ proṣitā lalitā sainyam jetu kāmena muhur kilakilā rābaiḥ ghoṣayantaḥ diśaḥ daśa sainyam ca lalitā devyāḥ sannaddham śāstra bhīṣaṇam pāśinyaḥ musalinyaḥ ca cakriṇyaḥ ca aparāḥ mune mudgariṇyaḥ paṭṭiśinyaḥ kodaṇḍinyaḥ tathā aparāḥ anekāḥ śaktayaḥ tīvrāḥ lalitā sainya saṃgatāḥ āyāta āyāta he duṣṭāḥ pāpinyaḥ vanitā adhamāḥ māyā parigrahaiḥ dūram mohayatyaḥ jaḍa āśayān śvasat bhujaga saṃkāśaiḥ bāṇaiḥ a tyanta bhīṣaṇaiḥ iti śaktīḥ bhartsayantaḥ dānavāḥ cakruḥ āhavam kācid ciccheda daitya indram kaṇṭhe paṭṭiśa pātanāt tatra lagnāḥ bahutarāḥ gṛdhrāḥ maṇḍala tām gatāḥ kācid śaktiḥ murārātim mukta śakti āyudham raṇe ekā tu gajam ārūḍhā kasyacid daitya durmateḥ uras sthale sva kariṇā vapra āghātam aśikṣayat kācid pratibhaṭa ārūḍham dantinam kumbha sīmani dhanuḥ daṇḍam dvidhā kṛtvā sva bhruvoḥ pratimām tanet śaktiḥ anyā śaraiḥ śātaiḥ śātayitvā virodhinaḥ kṛpāṇa padmā romālyām svakīyāyām mudam vyadhāt kācid mudgara pātena cūrṇayitvā virodhinaḥ abhyantaram śakti senā daityānām praviveśa ha praviveśa ca daityānām senā śakti bala antaram nīra kṣīra vat atyanta āśleṣam śakti suradviṣām saṃkula ākāra tām prāptaḥ yuddha kāle abhavat tadā śaktīnām khaḍga pātena lūna śuṇḍārada dvayāḥ daityānām kariṇaḥ mattāḥ mahā kroḍāḥ iva abhavan evam pravṛtte samare vīrāṇām ca bhayaṅkare aśakye smartum api antam kātara tvavatām nṛṇām bhīṣaṇānām bhīṣaṇe ca śastra vyāpāra durgame balāhakaḥ mahāgṛdhram vajra tīkṣṇa mukha ādikam kāla daṇḍa upamam jaṅghā kāṇḍe caṇḍa parākramam saṃhāragupta nāmānam pūrvam agre samutthitam dhūma vat dhūsara ākāram pakṣa kṣepa bhayaṃkaram pakṣau vitatya krośa ardham sa sthitaḥ bhīma niḥsvanaiḥ aṅgāra kuṇḍa vat cañcum vidārya abhakṣayat camūm saṃhāra guptam sa mahā gṛdhraḥ krūra vilocanaḥ balāhakam uvāha uccais ākṛṣṭa dhanuṣam raṇe balāhakaḥ vapuḥ dhunvan gṛdhra pṛṣṭha kṛta sthitiḥ sapakṣa kūṭa śaila sthaḥ balāhakaḥ iva abhavat sūcīmukhaḥ ca daitya indraḥ sūcī niṣṭhura pakṣatim kāka vāhanam āruhya kaṭhinam samaram vyadhāt mattaḥ parvata śṛṅga ābhaḥ cañcū daṇḍam samudvahan kāladaṇḍa pramāṇena jaṅghā kāṇḍena bhīṣaṇaḥ puṣkala āvartaka samā jambāla sadṛśa dyatiḥ krośa mātra āyatau pakṣau ubhau api samudvahan sūcīmukha adhiṣṭhitaḥ asau karaṭaḥ kaṭu vāsitaḥ mardayan cañcu ghātena śaktīnām maṇḍalam mahat atho phalamukhaḥ phālam gṛhītvā nijam āyudham vikarṇa ākhyaḥ ca daitya indraḥ camū bhartā mahā balaḥ bheruṇḍa patana ārūḍhaḥ pracaṇḍa yuddham ātanot vikaṭa ānana nāmānam vilasat paṭṭiśa āyudham uvāha samare caṇḍaḥ kukkuṭaḥ ati bhayaṃkaraḥ garjan kaṇṭha stha romāṇi harṣayan jvalat īkṣaṇaḥ paśyan puras śakti sainyam cacāla caraṇa āyudhaḥ karālākṣaḥ ca bhūbhartā ṣaṣṭhaḥ atyanta gariṣṭha daḥ vajra niṣṭhura ghoṣaḥ ca prācalat preta vāhanaḥ śmaśāna mantra śūreṇa tena saṃsādhitaḥ purā pretaḥ bhūta samāviṣṭaḥ tam uvāha raṇa ajire avāk mukhaḥ dīrgha bāhuḥ prasārita pada dvayaḥ protaḥ vāhana tām prāptaḥ karāla akṣam atha avahat anyaḥ karaṭakaḥ nāma daitya senā śikhāmaṇiḥ sardayāmāsa śaktīnām sainyam vetālavāhanaḥ yojana āyata mūrtiḥ san vetālaḥ krūra locanaḥ śmaśāna bhūmau vetālaḥ mantreṇa anena sādhitaḥ mardayāmāsa pṛtanām śaktīnām tena deśitaḥ bahudhā ayudhyata tadā śaktibhiḥ saha dānavaḥ evam ete khala ātmānaḥ sapta sapta arṇava upamāḥ śaktīnām sainikam tatra vyākulīcakruḥ uddhatāḥ tena dattaḥ varaḥ teṣām tapaḥ tuṣṭena bhāsvantā kaikaseyāḥ mahābhāgāḥ bhavatām tapasā adhunā parituṣṭaḥ asmi bhadram vaḥ bhavantaḥ vṛṇatām varam iti ukte dinanāthena kaikaseyāḥ tapaḥ kṛśāḥ prārthayāmāsuḥ atyartham durdāntam varam īdṛśam raṇeṣu sannidhātavyam asmākam netra kukṣiṣu tvayā yadā sannihitam tapana asmākam akṣiṣu tadā akṣi viṣayaḥ sarvaḥ niśceṣṭaḥ bhavatāt prabho tvad sānnidhya samiddhena netreṇa asmākam īkṣitāḥ tatas stabdheṣu śastreṣu vīkṣaṇāt eva naḥ prabho niśceṣṭāḥ ripavaḥ asmābhiḥ hantavyāḥ sukara tvāt iti pūrvam varaḥ prāptaḥ kaikaseyauḥ divākarāt atha sūrya samāviṣṭa netraiḥ teḥ tu nirīkṣitāḥ śaktayaḥ stabdha śastra oghāḥ viphala utsāḥ hatām gatāḥ viṣṭaṃbhita astra śastrāṇām śaktīnām na udyamaḥ abhavat abhibhūtāḥ sa niśvāsam śaktayaḥ joṣam āsata atha te vāsaram prāpya nānā praharaṇa udyatāḥ vyamardayan śakti sainyam daityāḥ sva svāmi deśitāḥ śaktayaḥ tāḥ tu sainyena nirvyāpārāḥ nirāyudhāḥ akṣubhyanta śaraiḥ teṣām vajra kaṅkaṭa bhodibhiḥ śaktayaḥ daitya śastra odhaiḥ viddha gātrāḥ sṛtāmṛjaḥ hāhākāram vitanvatyaḥ prapannāḥ laliteśvarīm cukruśuḥ śaktayaḥ sarvāḥ taiḥ staṃbhita nija āyudhāḥ atha devī ājñayā daṇḍanāthā pratyaṅga rakṣiṇī mahāmāyā samāruhya śaktīnām abhayam vyadhāt tamāla śyāmala ākārā śyāma kañcuka dhāriṇī śyāma chāye tamas lipte śyāma yukta turaṃgame vāsantī mohana abhikhyam dhanuḥ ādāya sa svanam siṃhanādam vinadya iṣūn avarṣat sarpa saṃnibhān kṛṣṇa rūpa bhujaṃga bhān adhas musala saṃnibhān mohana astra viniṣṭhyūtān bāṇān daityāḥ na sehire itas tatas mardyamānāḥ mahā māyā śilīmukhaiḥ prakopam paramam prāptāḥ balāhaka mukhāḥ khalāḥ atho tiraskaraṇī ambā daṇḍanāthā nideśataḥ andha abhidham mahā astram sā mumoca dviṣatām gaṇe balāhaka ādyāḥ te sapta dinanātha vara uddhatāḥ andha astreṇa nijam netram dadhire chāditam yathā udgatena andha bāṇena cakṣuḥ teṣām vyadhīyata andhīkṛtāḥ ca te sapta na tu praikṣanta kiñcana tad vīkṣaṇasya virahāt śastra stambhaḥ kṣayam gataḥ punar sa siṃhanādam tāḥ prodyata āyudha pāṇayaḥ cakruḥ samara sannāham daityānām prajighāṃsayā tiraskaraṇikām devīm agre kṛtvā mahā balām sat upāya prasaṅgeṇa bhṛśam tuṣṭāḥ raṇam vyadhuḥ sādhu sādhu mahābhāge tiraskaraṇikā aṃbike sthāne kṛta tiraskārāḥ dvipām eṣām durātmanām tvam hi durjana netrāṇām tiraskāra mahā oṣadhī tvayā baddha dṛśā anena daitya cakreṇa bhūyate asmādṛśām ajayyeṣu yadā eṣu vyasanam kṛtam tat tvayā eva durācārān etān sapta mahā asurān nihatān lalitā śrutvā saṃtoṣam param āpsyati evam tvayā viracite daṇḍinī prīti māpsyati mantriṇī api mahābhāgāyāḥ eva parām mudam tasmāt tvam eva sapta etān nigṛhaṇa raṇa ajire eṣām sainyam tu nikhilam nāśayāmaḥ udāyudhāḥ tām āyāntam samāvekṣya te sapta atha sura adhamāḥ praviṣṭam api sāvitram na aśakam tad nirodhane mahā bala parākramam astreṇa ca ruṣā ca andham balāhaka mahā asuram mākṛṣya keśeṣu asinā cakarta antardhi devatā tasya vāhana gṛdhrasya lunānā patriṇā śiraḥ sūcīmukhasya abhimukham tiraskaraṇikā vrajat tasya paṭṭiśa pātena vilūya kaṭhinam śiraḥ anyeṣām api pañcānām pañcatvam akarot śanais taiḥ sapta daitya muṇḍaiḥ ca grathita anyonya keśakaiḥ hāra dāma gale kṛtvā nanāda antardhi devatā hatvā tad rakta salilaiḥ bahvīḥ prāvāhayat nadīḥ tatra āścaryam abhūt bhūri māhāmāya aṃbikā kṛtam balāhaka ādi senā nyām dṛṣṭi rodhana vaibhavāt hata śiṣṭāḥ katipayāḥ bahu vitrāsa saṅkulāḥ śaraṇam jagmuḥ ati ārtāḥ krandantam śūnyakeśvaram daṇḍinīm ca mahāmāyām praśaṃsanti muhur muhur prasādam aparam cakṣuḥ tasyāḥ ādāyapipriyuḥ sādhu sādhu iti tatrasthāḥ śaktayaḥ kampa maulayaḥ tiraskaraṇikām devīm aślāghanta pade pade iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne balāhakādisaptasenāpativadhaḥ nāma caturviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ tatas śrutvā vadham teṣām tapaḥ balavatām api nyaśvasat kṛṣṇa sarpa indraḥ iva bhaṇḍaḥ mahā asuraḥ bhaṇḍaḥ pracaṇḍa śaiṇḍīryaḥ kāṅkṣamāṇaḥ raṇe jayam yuvarājaḥ api sa krodhaḥ viṣaṅgeṇa yavīyasā bhaṇḍāsuram namaskṛtya mantra sthānam upāgamat atyāptaiḥ mantribhiḥ yuktaḥ kuṭila akṣa puraḥsaraiḥ lalitāvijaye mantram cakāra kvathita āśyaḥ uvāca aho bata kula bhraṃśaḥ samāyātaḥ suradviṣām upekṣām adhunā kartum pravṛttaḥ balavān vidhiḥ tādṛśāṇām iha naḥ āgataḥ ayam viparyayaḥ dīrgha āyuṣam anāyuṣkam durdhātā bhavitavya tā kva sattvam asmat bāhunām kva iyam durlalitā vadhūḥ akāṇḍaḥ eva vidhinā kṛtaḥ ayam niṣṭhuraḥ vidhiḥ śauryayā adhi saṃgrāma bhū cakre senānyaḥ vinipātitāḥ evam uddāma darpa āḍhyā vanitā kā api māyinī imam prasaṃgam vaktum ca jihvā jihvā iti māmakī mayā cāra mukhāt jñātā tasyāḥ vṛttiḥ mahā balā sarveṣām api sainyānām paścāt eva avatiṣṭhate asmin eva hi avasare pārṣṇigrāhaḥ vidhīyatām pārṣṇigraham imam kartum viṣaṅgaḥ caturaḥ bhavet tena prauḍha mada unmatāḥ bahu saṃgrāma durmadāḥ daśa pañca ca senānyaḥ saha yāntu yuyutsayā pṛṣṭhatas parivārāḥ tu na tathā santi te punar atas tvam bahu sannāham āvidhāya mada utkaṭaḥ viṣaṅga gupta rūpeṇa pārṣṇigrāham samācara alpīyasī tvayā sārddham senā gacchatu vikramāt sajjāḥ ca lantu senānyaḥ dikpāla vijaya uddhatāḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ ca senānām daśa pañca calantu te tvam gupta veṣaḥ tām duṣṭām sannipatya dṛḍham jahi sā eva niḥśeṣa śaktīnām mūla bhūtā mahīyasī tasyāḥ sa mūla nāśena śakti vṛndam vinaśyati sarveṣām eva paścāt yaḥ rathaḥ calati bhāsuraḥ vahat muhar vījyamānam cāmarāṇām catuṣṭayam uttaṅga ketu saṃghāta likhita ambuda maṇḍalaḥ tasmin rathe samāyāti sā dṛṣṭā hariṇa īkṣaṇā nibṛtam saṃnipatya tvam cihnena anena lakṣitām tām vijitya durācārām keśa iṣvā kṛṣya mardaya puratas calite sainye sattva śālini sā vadhūḥ bhavat sahāya bhūtāyām senā indrāṇām iha abhidhā puṇḍraketuḥ ca caṇḍabāhuḥ ca kukkuraḥ jambukākṣaḥ jambhanaḥ ca tīkṣṇaśṛṅgaḥ trikaṇṭakaḥ candraguptaḥ ca pañca ete daśa ca uktāḥ camū varāḥ eka eka akṣauhiṇī yuktāḥ pratyekam bhavatā saha balāḥ tathā gupta samācāraḥ pārṣṇigrāham samācara hanta viṣaṅgam preṣayāmāsa rakṣitam sainyapālakaiḥ atha śrī lalitā devyāḥ pārṣṇigrāha kṛta udyame andhakāraḥ samabhavat tasya bāhya cikīrṣayā nīlakaṇṭha nibha chāyam nibiḍam paprathe tamaḥ kuñjeṣu piṇḍitam iva pradhāvat iva saṃdhiṣu ujjihānam iva kṣoṇī vivarebhyaḥ sahasraśas kvacid dīpa prabhā jāle kṛta kātara ceṣṭitam datta avalambanam iva strīṇām karṇa utpala tviṣi kṛta priya āśleṣam iva sphurantīṣu asi yaṣṭiṣu gupta praviṣṭam iva ca śyāmāsu vana paṅktiṣu krameṇa bahulībhūtam prasasāra mahattamaḥ triyāmā vāma nayanā nīla kañcuka rociṣā timireṇa āvṛtam viśvam na kiñcid pratyapadyata asurāṇām praduṣṭānām rātriḥ eva bala āvahā teṣām māyā vilāsaḥ ayam tasyām eva hi vardhate atha pracalitam sainyam viṣaṅgeṇa mahā ojasā dhauta khaḍga latā chāyā vardhiṣṇu timira chaṭam damana ādyāḥ ca senānyaḥ śmāma kaṅkaṭa dhāriṇaḥ śyāma uṣṇīṣa dharāḥ śyāma varṇa sarva paricchadāḥ eka tvam iva saṃprāptāḥ timireṇa ati bhūyasā viṣaṅgam anusaṃceluḥ kṛta agraja namaskṛtim kūṭena yuddha kṛtyena vijigīṣuḥ maheśvarīm meghaḍambarakam nāma dadhe vakṣasi kaṅkaṭam yathā tasya niśā yuddha anurūpaḥ veṣa saṃgrahaḥ tathā kṛtavatī senā śyāmalam kañcuka ādikam paṇava ānaka bherīṇām na ca ghoṣa vijṛṃbhaṇam gupta ācārāḥ pracalitāḥ timireṇa samāvṛtāḥ paraiḥ adṛśya gatayaḥ viṣkośīkṛta riṣṭayaḥ paścima abhimukham yānti lalitāyāḥ patākinīm āvṛta uttara mārgeṇa pūrva bhāgam aśiśriyan sa avadhānāḥ pracalitāḥ pārṣṇigrāhāya dānavāḥ bhūyas purasya digbhāgam gatvā manda parākramāḥ āgatya nibhṛtam pṛṣṭhe kavaca channa vigrahāḥ apaśyan ati dīptābhiḥ śaktibhiḥ parivāritam sahasra āditya saṃkāśām paścima abhimukhām sthitām kāma īśvarā ādi nityābhiḥ sva samāna samṛddhibhiḥ tām tathā bhūta vṛttāntām a tādṛśa raṇa udyamām purogatam mahat sainyam vīkṣamāṇa sa kautukam manvānaḥ ca hi tām eva viṣaṅgaḥ su durāśayaḥ pṛṣṭhavaṃśe ratha indrasya ghaṭṭayāmāsa sainikaiḥ mā ādi śaktīnām parivāra varūthinī mahā kalakalam cakruḥ aṇima ādyāḥ paraḥśatam paṭṭiśaiḥ drughaṇaiḥ ca eva bhindipālaiḥ bhuśuṇḍibhiḥ kaṭhora vajra nirdhāta niṣṭhuraiḥ śakti maṇḍalaiḥ ākasmika raṇa utsāha viparyāviṣṭa vigraham akāṇḍa kṣubhitam ca āsīt ratha stham śakti maṇḍalam vipāṭaiḥ pāṭayāmāsuḥ adṛśyaiḥ andhakāriṇaḥ adṛśyamāna śastrāṇām adṛśya nija varmaṇām timira channa rūpāṇām dānavānām śilīmukhaiḥ śaktīnām maṇḍalam tene krandanam lalitām prati karṇa ākarṇikayā ākarṇya lalitā kopam ādadhe etasmin antare bhaṇḍaḥ caṇḍa durmatri paṇḍitaḥ daśa akṣauhiṇikā yuktam kuṭila akṣam mahā ojasam lalitā sainya nāśāya yuddhāya prajighāya saḥ yathā paścāt kalakalam śrutvā agrevartinī camūḥ na āgacchati tathā cakre kuṭilākṣaḥ mahā raṇam atyanta tumulam ca āsīt śaktīnām sainike mahat naktasattvāḥ ca daitya indrāḥ timireṇa samāvṛtāḥ itas tatas śithila tām kaṇṭake ninyuḥ uddhatāḥ niṣaṅgeṇa durāśeṇa dhamana ādyaiḥ camū varaiḥ camūbhiḥ ca praṇahitāḥ nyapatan śatru koṭayaḥ tābhiḥ daitya astra mālābhiḥ cakrarāja rathaḥ vṛtaḥ baka āvali nibiḍāt śailarājaḥ iva ābabhau ākrānta parvaṇā adhastāt viṣaṅgeṇa durātmanā muktaḥ ekaḥ śaraḥ devyāḥ tālavṛntam acūrṇayat atha tena avyāhitena saṃbhrānte śakti maṇḍale kāmeśvarī mukhāḥ nityāḥ mahantam krodham āyayuḥ īṣat bhṛkuṭī saṃsaktam śrī devyāḥ vadana ambujam nityā kāla svarūpiṇyaḥ pratyekam tithi vigrahāḥ praṇipatya ca tām devīm mahā rājñīm mahodayām ūcuḥ vācam akāṇḍa utthām yuddha kautuka gadgadām devadevī mahā rājñī tava agre brekṣitām camūm daṇḍinī mantranātha ādi mahā śakti ābha pālitām kātarāḥ duṣṭāḥ māyā chadma parāyaṇāḥ pārṣṇigrāhena yuddhena bādhante ratha puṃgavam tasmāt timira saṃchanna mūrtīnām vibudha druhām śamayāmaḥ vayam darpam kṣaṇa mātram vilokaya yā vahni vāsinī nityā yā jvālā mālinī parā tābhyām pradīpite yuddhe draṣṭum śaktāḥ praśamayya mahā darpam pārṣṇigrāha pravartinām sahasā eva āgamiṣyāmaḥ sevitum śrī pada ambujam mahā rājñi mardana artham durātmanām atha kāmeśvarī nityā praṇamya laliteśvarīm tayā saṃpreṣitā tābhiḥ kuṇḍalīkṛta kārmukā sā hantum tān durācārān kūṭa yuddha kṛtakṣaṇān bāla aruṇam iva krodha aruṇam vaktram vitanvatī pāpiṣṭhāḥ māyā niṣṭhāḥ chinadmi vaḥ andhakāram anuprāpya kūṭa yuddha parāyaṇāḥ iti tān bhartsayantī sā tūṇīra utkhāta sāyakāt sajja kārmuka hastāḥ ca bhaga mālā puraḥsarāḥ anyāḥ ca caritāḥ nityāḥ kṛta parva avarohaṇāḥ mālini nityā ca yā nityā vahni vāsinī atha te duṣṭa danujāḥ pradīpte yuddha maṇḍale prakāśa vapuṣaḥ tatra mara antam krodham āyayuḥ kāmeśvarī ādikāḥ nityāḥ tāḥ pañcadaśa sa āyudhāḥ sa siṃhanādāḥ tān daityān amṛdnan eva helayā tāḥ ca nitya avalat kvāṇa kaṅkaṇaiḥ yudhi pāṇibhiḥ ākṛṣya prāma kodaṇḍāḥ tenire yuddham uddhatam nityānām niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ ca saṃhṛtāḥ jaghāna damanam duṣṭam kāmeśī prathamam śaraiḥ dīrghajihvam camū nātham bhaga mālā vyadārat kaklasam vahnivāsāḥ ca nijaghāna śaraiḥ śataiḥ mahā vajra īśvarā bāṇaiḥ abhinat kekivāhanam puklasam śivadūtī ca prāhiṇot yama sādanam puṇḍra ketum bhuja uddaṇḍam tvaritā samadārayat kulasundarikā nityā caṇḍabāhum ca kukkuram jambukākṣam jṛṃbhaṇam ca vyatanvātām raṇe balim sarva maṅgalikā nityā tīkṣṇa śṛṅgam akhaṇḍayat yā jvālā mālinikā nityā jaghāna ugram tri karṇakam candraguptam ca duḥśīlam citram citrā vyadārat senā nātheṣu sarveṣu nihateṣu durātmasu viṣaṅgaḥ paramaḥ kuddhaḥ cacāla puratas balī atha yāma avaśeṣāyām yāminyām ghaṭikā dvayam nityābhiḥ saha saṃgrāmam vidhāya sa durāśayaḥ kāmeśvarī kara ākṛṣṭa cāpa utthauḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhinna varmā dṛḍhataram viṣaṅgaḥ vihvala āśayaḥ hata avaśiṣṭaiḥ yodhaiḥ ca sārdham eva palāyitaḥ tābhiḥ na nihataḥ duṣṭaḥ yasmāt vadhyaḥ sa dānavaḥ daṇḍanātha śareṇa eva kāla daṇḍa sama tviṣā tasmin palāyite duṣṭe viṣaṅge bhaṇḍa sodare sā vibhātā ca rajanī prasannāḥ ca abhavan diśaḥ iti tāḥ samarāt nityāḥ tasmin kāle vyaraṃsiṣuḥ nityāḥ śrī lalitām devīm praṇipetuḥ jaya uddhatāḥ nityānām rūpa jālam ca śastra kṣatam alokayat śrutvā udantam mahā rājñī kṛpā apāṅgena sā aikṣata tad ālokana mātreṇa vraṇaḥ nirvraṇa tām agāt nityānām vikramaiḥ ca api lalitā prītim āsadat iti śrī brahmāṇḍa mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalitā upākhyāne viṣaṅgapalāyanam nāma pañcaviṃśaḥ adhyāya daśa akṣauhiṇikā yuktaḥ kuṭilākṣaḥ api vīryavān daṇḍanātha śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ raṇe bhagnaḥ palāyitaḥ daśa ākṣauhiṇikam sainyam tayā rātrau vināśitam imam vṛttāntam ākarṇya bhaṇḍaḥ kṣobham atha āyayau rātrau kapaṭa saṃgrāmam duṣṭānām nirjara druhām mantriṇī daṇḍanāthā ca śrutvā nirvedam āpatuḥ mahā cakra ratha indrasya na jātam rakṣaṇam balaiḥ etam tu avasaram prāpya rātrau duṣṭaiḥ parākṛtam kaḥ vṛttāntaḥ abhavat tatra svāminyā kim raṇaḥ kṛtaḥ vimraṣṭavyam idam kāryam pravṛttiḥ tatra kīdṛśā mahādevyāḥ ca hṛdaye kaḥ prasaṅgaḥ pravartate iti śaṅkā ākulāḥ tatra daṇḍanāthā purogamāḥ mantriṇīm puratas kṛtvā praceluḥ lalitām prati śakti cakra camū nāthāḥ sarvāḥ tāḥ pūjitāḥ drutam vyatītāyām vibhāvaryām ratha indram paryavārayan avaruhya sva yānābhyām mantriṇī daṇḍa nāyike abhajetām mahā rājñīm mantriṇī daṇḍa nāyike te vyajijñapatām devyāḥ aṣṭāṅga spṛṣṭa bhū tale mahā pramādaḥ samabhūt iti naḥ śrutam aṃbike kūṭa yuddha prakāreṇa daityaiḥ apakṛtam khalaiḥ sa durātmā durācāraḥ prakāśa samārāt trasan daivāt naḥ svāminī gātre duṣṭānām amara druhām śara ādika parāmarśaḥ na jātaḥ tena jīvati eka avalambanam kṛtvā mahā rājñi bhavat padam vayam sarvāḥ hi jīvāmaḥ sādhayāmaḥ samīhitam atas asmābhiḥ prakartavyam śrīmatī aṅgasya rakṣaṇam jetavyāḥ bhaṇḍa ādyāḥ dānava adhamāḥ kūṭa yuddham na kurvanti na viśanti camūm imām tathā mahendra śailasya kāryam dakṣiṇa deśataḥ bahu vistāram yojanānām śata avadhi bahli prākāra valayam rakṣaṇa artham vidhīyatām mad senā niveśasya dviṣām darpa śamāya ca yatas dakṣiṇa deśa stham śūnyakam vidviṣām puram dvāre ca bahavaḥ kalpyāḥ parivārāḥ udāyudhāḥ nirgacchatām praviśatām janānām uparodhakāḥ anālasyāḥ anidrāḥ ca vidheyāḥ satata udyatāḥ evam ca sati duṣṭānām kūṭa yuddham cikīrṣitam avelāsu ca saṃdhyāsu madhyarātriṣu ca dviṣām aśakyam eva bhavati prauḍham ākramaṇam haṭhāt no ced durāśayāḥ daityāḥ bahu māyā parigrahāḥ mantriṇyāḥ daṇḍanāthāyāḥ iti śrutvā vacaḥ tadā śuci danta rucā muktā vahantī lalitā bravīt bhavatīnām ayam mantraḥ cāru buddhyā vicāritaḥ ayam kuśala dhī mārgaḥ nītiḥ eṣā sanātanī sva cakrasya puras rakṣām vidhāya dṛḍha sādhanaiḥ para cakra ākramaḥ kāryaḥ jigīṣadbhiḥ mahājanaiḥ iti uktvā mantriṇī daṇḍanāthe sā laliteśvarī nityām āhūya idam uvāca ha vatse tvam vahni rūpā asi jvālā mālā maya ākṛtiḥ tvayā vidhīyatām rakṣā balasya asya mahīyasaḥ triṃśat yojanam unnaddham jvālā ākāra tvam āvraja iti uktvā mantriṇī daṇḍanāthe sā laliteśvarī sā ca nitya anitya mayī jvalat jvā lāmaya ākṛtiḥ caturdaśī tithi mayī tathā iti praṇanāma tām kuṇḍalīkṛtya jajvāla śāla rūpeṇa sā punar nabhaḥ valaya jambāla jvālā mālā maya ākṛtiḥ babhāse daṇḍanāthāyāḥ mantri nātha camūḥ api balam mahā udaram sālam praviveśa gata klamā rāja cakra ratha indram tu madhye saṃsthāpya daṇḍinī vāma pakṣe ratham svīyam dakṣiṇe śyāmalā ratham paścāt bhāge sampadeśīm purastāḥ ca haya āsanām dvāre niveśayāmāsa viṃśati akṣauhiṇī yutām yad daṇḍa āyudha udagrām stambhinīm nāma devatām yā devī daṇḍanāthāyāḥ vighnadevī iti viśrutā evam su rakṣitam kṛtvā śibiram yotriṇī tathā pūṣaṇi udita bhūyiṣṭhe punar yuddham upāśrayat kṛtvā kilakilā rāvam tatas śakti mahā camūḥ agni prākāraka dvārāt nirjagām mahā ravā ittham su rakṣitam śrutvā lalitā śibira udaram bhūyas saṃjvaram āpannaḥ pracaṇḍaḥ bhaṇḍa dānavaḥ viṣaṅgeṇa viśukreṇa asamam ātma sutaiḥ api caturān yuddha kṛtyeṣu samāhūya sa dānavaḥ preṣayāmāsa yuddhāya bhaṇḍaḥ caṇḍa krudhā jvalan triṃśat saṃkhyāḥ ca tad putrāḥ mahā kāyāḥ mahā balāḥ teṣām nāmāni vakṣyāmi samākarṇaya kumbhajaiḥ catur bāhuḥ cakora akṣaḥ tṛtīyaḥ tu catuḥ śirāḥ vajra ghoṣaḥ ca ūrdhva keśaḥ mahā kāyaḥ mahā hanuḥ makhaśatruḥ makhaskandī siṃhaghoṣaḥ sirālakaḥ laḍunaḥ paṭṭasenaḥ ca purājit pūrva mārakaḥ svargaśatruḥ svargabalaḥ durga ākhyaḥ svargakaṇṭakaḥ atimāyaḥ bṛhat māyaḥ upamāyaḥ ca vīryavān pituḥ sadṛśa dos vīryāḥ pituḥ sadṛśa vigrahāḥ āgatya bhaṇḍa caraṇau abhyavandata bhaktitaḥ tān udvīkṣya prasannābhyām locanābhyām sa dānavaḥ sa gauravam idam vākyam babhāṣe kula ghātakaḥ bho bho madīyāḥ tanayāḥ bhavatām kaḥ samaḥ bhuvi bhavatām eva satyena jitam viśvam mayā purā śakrasya agneḥ yamasya api nirṛteḥ pāśinaḥ tathā kaceṣu karṣaṇam kopāt kṛtam yuṣmābhiḥ āhave astrāṇi api ca śastrāṇi jānītha nikhilāni api jāgratsu eva hi yuṣmāsu kula bhraṃśaḥ ayam āgataḥ māyāvinī dulalitā kācid strī yuddha durmadā bahubhiḥ sva samānābhiḥ strībhiḥ yuktā hinasti naḥ tat enām samare avaśyam ātma vaśyām vidhāsyatha jīva grāham ca sā grāhyā bhavadbhiḥ jvalat āyudhaiḥ aprameya prakopa andhān vaḥ ekām striyam prati sampreṣaṇam anaucityam tathā api eṣa vidheḥ kramaḥ iti uktvā bhaṇḍa daitya indraḥ tān prahaiṣīt raṇam prati dviśatam ca akṣauhiṇīnām tad sahāya tayā ahinot dviśati akṣauhiṇī senā mukhyasya tilakāyitā baddha bhrukuṭayaḥ śastra pāṇayaḥ niryayuḥ gṛhāt nirgame bhaṇḍa putrāṇām bhūḥ prakampam alambata utpātāḥ vividhāḥ jātāḥ vitrastam ca abhavat jagant tān kumārān mahāsattvān lāja varṣaiḥ avākiran yānaiḥ calitān paura vṛddha purandhrayaḥ bandinaḥ māgadhāḥ ca eva kumārāṇām stutim vyadhuḥ maṅgala ārārtikam cakruḥ dvāre dvāre pura aṅganāḥ bhidyamānā iva vasudhā kṛṣyamāṇam iva abaram āsīt teṣām viniryāṇe ghūrṇamānaḥ iva arṇavaḥ dviśati akṣauhiṇī senām gṛhītvā śakti sainyāni sarvāṇi bhakṣayāmaḥ kṣaṇāt raṇe teṣām āyudha cakrāṇi cūrṇayāmaḥ śita aiśaraiḥ agni prākāra valayam śamayāmaḥ ca raṃhasā durvidagdhām tām lalitām bandīkurmaḥ ca sarvaram iti anyonyam pravalgantaḥ vīra bhāṣaṇa ghoṣaṇaiḥ sūnavaḥ yauvanena madena andhāḥ bhūyasā ruddha dṛṣṭayaḥ bhrukuṭi kuṭilāḥ cakruḥ siṃhanādam mahāttaram vidīrṇam iva tena āsīt brahmāṇḍaiḥ caṇḍima spṛśā utpāta vārida utsṛṣṭa ghora nirghāta raṃhasā etasya ananubhūtasya mahā śabdasya ḍambaraḥ kṣobhayāmāsa śaktīnām śravāṃsi ca manāṃsi ca catur bāhu makhān bhūtvā māgatān yuddha kṛtyāya bālā kautūhalam dadhe kumārī lalitā devyāḥ tasyāḥ nikaṭa vāsinī samasta śakti cakrāṇām pūjya vikramaśālinī lalitā sadṛśa ākārā kumārī kopam ādadhe yā sadā nava varṣā iva sarva vidyā mahā khaniḥ bāla aruṇa tanuḥ śroṇī śoṇa varṇa vapuḥ latā mahā rājñī pāda pīṭhe nityam āhita saṃnidhiḥ tasyāḥ bahis carāḥ prāṇāḥ yā caturtham vilocanam tān āgatān bhaṇḍa sutān saṃhariṣyāmi sa tvaram iti niścitya bāla ambā mahā rājñyai vyajijñapat mātarbhaṇḍa mahā daitya sūnavaḥ yoddhum āgatāḥ saphurantau iva mama bāhū yuddha kaṇḍūyayā anayā krīḍā mama eṣā hantavyā na bhavatyā nivāraṇaiḥ aham hi vālikā nityam krīḍaneṣu anurāgiṇī yāsyāmi ca etasā iti vijñāpitā devī pratyuvāca kumārikām vatse tvam ati mṛdu aṅgī nava varṣā nava kramā navīna yuddha śikṣā ca kumārī tvam mama aikikā tvām vinā kṣaṇa mātram me na niśvāsaḥ pravartate daṇḍinī mantriṇī ca eva śaktayaḥ anyāḥ ca koṭiśas iti śrī lalitā devyā niruddhā api kumārikā kaumāra kautuka āviṣṭā punar yuddham ayācata su dṛḍham niścayam dṛṣṭvā tasyāḥ śrī lalitā ambikā anujñām kṛtavatī eva gāḍham āśliṣya bāhubhiḥ karṇīratham mahā rājñyā cāpa daṇḍāt samuddhṛtam tasyām raṇe pravṛttāyām sarva parva stha devatāḥ baddha añjali puṭāḥ nemuḥ pradhṛta asi paraṃparāḥ tābhiḥ praṇamyamānā sā cakrarāja ratha uttamāt tām āyāntam atho dṛṣṭvā kumārīm kopa pāṭalām mantriṇī daṇḍanāthe ca sa bhaye vācam ūcatuḥ kim bhartṛ dārike yuddhe vyavasāyaḥ kṛtaḥ tvayā akāṇḍe kim mahā rājñyā preṣitā asi raṇam prati tvam mūrtam jīvitam asi śrī devyāḥ bālike yatas nivartasva raṇa utsāhāt praṇāmaḥ te vidhīyate iti tābhyām prārthitā api prācalat dṛḍha niścayā atyantam vismaya āviṣṭe mantriṇī daṇḍa nāyike saha eva tasyāḥ rakṣā artham celatuḥ pārśvayoḥ dvayoḥ atha agnivaraṇa dvārā tābhyām anugatā satī prabhūta senā yuktābhyām nirjagāma kumārikā sa nātha śakti senānām sarvāsām anugṛhṇatī praṇāma añjali jālāni karṇīratha kṛta āsanā tanayān duṣṭān abhyadravat ariṃdamā tasyāḥ prādeśikam sainyam kumāryāḥ na hi vidyate bhaṇḍāsura kumāraiḥ taiḥ mahā rājñī kumārikā atyanta vismitāḥ daitya kumārāḥ nava varṣiṇīm karmīratha sthām ālokya kiranti iṃśara maṇḍalam tad īkṣaṇe bālikayā kriyamāṇam mahā raṇam vyajijñapat mahā rājñyai bhramatyaḥ paricārikāḥ mantriṇī daṇḍanāthe ca na tām vijahatuḥ raṇe prekṣaka tva m anuprāpte tṛṣṇīm eva babhūvatuḥ sarveṣām daitya putrāṇām eka rūpā kumārikā pratyeka bhinnā dadṛśe biṃba mālā iva bhāsvantaḥ sāyakaiḥ agni cūḍālaiḥ teṣām marmāṇi bhindatī āścaryam bruvataḥ vyomni paśyatām tridivaukasām sādhuvādaiḥ bahuvidhaiḥ matriṇī daṇḍanāthayoḥ arcyamānā raṇam cakre laghu hastā kumārikā prakāśayāmāsa balam lalitā duhitā nijam mahā rājñī kumārikā dviśati akṣauhiṇī sainyam bhasmasātkarot kṣaṇāt akṣauhiṇīnām kṣayataḥ kṣaṇāt kopam upāgatāḥ ākṛṣṭa guru dhanvānaḥ te apatan eka helayā tatas kalakale jāte śaktīnām ca divaukasām yugapad triṃśataḥ bāṇān asṛjat sā kumārikā hasta lāghavam āśritya muktaiḥ candra ardha sāyakaiḥ triṃśatā triṃśataḥ sāhatam śiraḥ iti bhaṇḍasya putreṣu prāpteṣu yama sādanam atyanta vismaya āviṣṭāḥ vabṛṣuḥ puṣpam abhragāḥ sā ca putrī mahā rājñyāḥ vidhvasta asura mainikā mantriṇī daṇḍanāthābhyām āliṅgyata bhṛśam mudā tasyāḥ parākrama unmeṣaiḥ nṛtyanti ojaya dāyibhiḥ sarvāḥ ca daṇḍa nāthā puraḥsarāḥ tat āścaryam mahā rājñyai nivedayitum udgatāḥ tābhiḥ nivedyamānāni sā devī lalitā ambikā putrī bhuja avadānāni śrutvā prītim samāyayau samastam api tat cakram śaktīnām tad parākramaiḥ a dṛṣṭa pūrvaiḥ deveṣu vismayasya vaśam gatam iti śrī brahmāṇḍe mahāpurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalita upākhyāne bhaṇḍaputravadhaḥ nāma ṣaḍviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha naṣṭeṣu putreṣu śoka anala pariplutaḥ hā putrāḥ hā guṇa udārāḥ hā mad eka parāyaṇāḥ hā mad netra sudhā pūrāḥ hā mad kula vivardhanāḥ samasta suraśreṣṭha mada bhañjana tatparāḥ samasta sura strīṇām antar mohana manmathāḥ diśata prīti vācam me mama aṅke valgata adhunā kim idānīm imam tātam avamucya sukham gatāḥ yuṣmān vinā na śobhante mama rājyāni putrakāḥ katham evam viniḥśeṣam hatāḥ ayūyam durāśayāḥ apradhṛṣya bhujā sattvān bhavataḥ mad kula aṅkurān katham eka pade duṣṭā vanitā saṃgare avadhīt mama naṣṭāni saukhyāni mama naṣṭāḥ kulastriyaḥ itas param kule kṣīṇe sāhasāni sukhāni ca bhavataḥ sukṛtaiḥ labdhvā mama pūrva janus kṛtaiḥ nāśaḥ ayam bhavatām adya jātaḥ naṣṭaḥ tatas asmi aham mūrchayā lupta hṛdayaḥ niṣpapāta nu pāsanāt viśukraḥ ca viṣaṅgaḥ ca kuṭilākṣaḥ ca saṃsadi bhaṇḍam āśvāsayāmāsuḥ daivasya kuṭila kramaiḥ uvāca devaki prākṛtaḥ iva prāptaḥ śokasya vaśya tām dharmavān vihitaḥ panthāḥ vīrāṇām eṣa śāśvataḥ etat eva vināśāya śalya vat bādhate manaḥ yat strī samāgatya haṭhāt ni hanti su bhaṭān raṇe bhaṇḍena caṇḍa kālāgni sadṛśaḥ krodhaḥ ādadhe mahā akṣi yugalaḥ bhṛśam jajvāla tejasā idānīm eva tām duṣṭām khaḍgena anena khaṇḍaśas śakalīkṛtya samare śramam prāpsyāmi bandhubhiḥ tam nirudhya ca saṃbhrāntāḥ sarve dānava puṃgavāḥ na tad arthe tvayā kāryaḥ svāmin saṃbhramaḥ īdṛśaḥ bhavat ājñā lavam prāpya samasta bhuvanam haṭhāt vimardayitum īśāḥ smaḥ kimu tām mugdha bhāminīm kim cūṣayāmaḥ sapta abdhīn kṣodayāmaḥ atha vā girīn chinadāma surān sarvān bhinadāma tad ālayān pinṣāma haritpālān ājñām dehi mahāmate iti udīrita mā ākarṇya mahā ahaṅkāra garvitam uvāca vacanam kruddhaḥ pratigha aruṇa locanaḥ viśukra bhavatā gatvā mā ayās anta arhita varṣmaṇā jaya vighnam mahā yantram karttavyam kaṭake dviṣām iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā viśukraḥ roṣa rūṣitaḥ paryasta kiraṇa stoma pāṭalī kṛta diṅmukhaḥ anurāgavatī saṃdhyā prayāntam bhānumālinam carama abdheḥ iva payas kaṇāḥ tārāḥ virejire māyā ratham samārūḍhaḥ gūḍha śarvara saṃvṛtaḥ adṛśya vapūḥ āpede lalitā kaṭakam khalaḥ tatra gatvā jvalat jvālam vahni prākāra maṇḍalam paritas vibhraman śālam avakāśam avāpnuvan dakṣiṇam dvāram āsādya nidadhyau kṣaṇam uddhataḥ tatra apaśyat mahāsattvāḥ sa avadhānāḥ dhṛta āyudhāḥ mārūḍha yānāḥ sa naddha varmāṇaḥ dvāra deśataḥ stambhinī pramukhāḥ śaktīḥ viśati akṣauhiṇī yutāḥ sarvadā dvāra rakṣā artham nirdiṣṭā daṇḍanāthayā vilokya vismaya āviṣṭaḥ vicārya ca ciram tadā aṣṭa dikṣu aṣṭa śūlena saṃhāra akṣara maulinā alasā kṛpaṇā dīnā nitandrā ca pramīlikā klībā ca nirahaṅkārā ca iti aṣṭau devatāḥ smṛtāḥ devatā aṣṭakam etas ca śūla aṣṭaka puṭa upari pūjām vidhāya mantrasya balibhiḥ chāgala ādibhiḥ tat yantram ca ari kaṭake prākṣipat samare asuraḥ papāta kaṭaka antare vimukta śastra saṃnyāsam āsthitāḥ dīna mānasāḥ kim hataiḥ asuraiḥ kāryam śastra aśastri kramaiḥ alam phalam kim vā prāṇi hiṃsā ca pāpa dā amarāṇām kṛte kaḥ ayam kim asmākam bhaviṣyati vṛthak kalakalam kṛtvā na phalam yuddha karmaṇā kā svāminī mahā rājñī kā vā asau daṇḍanāyikā kā vā sā mantriṇī śyāmā bhṛtya tvam naḥ atha kīdṛśam iha sarvābhiḥ asmābhiḥ bhṛtya bhūta abhirekikā vanitā svāminī kṛtye kim phalam mokṣyate param yuddham śāmyatu ca naḥ deha śastra kṣati pradam yuddhe ca maraṇam bhāvi vṛthak syuḥ jīvitāni naḥ utsāhena phalam nā asti nidrā eva ekā sukha āvahā na asti citta viśrānti dāyakam etādṛśīḥ ca naḥ jñātvā sā rājñī kim kariṣyati tasyāḥ rājñī tvam api naḥ samavāyena kalpitam evam ca upekṣitā asmābhiḥ sā vinaṣṭa balā bhavet naṣṭa sattvā ca sā rājñī kān mama śikṣām kariṣyati evam eva raṇa āraṃbham vimucya vidhuta āyudhāḥ śaktayaḥ nidrayā dvāre ghūrṇamānāḥ iva abhavan sarvatra māndyam kāryeṣu mahat ālasyam āgatam śithilam ca abhavat sarvam śaktīnām kaṭakam mahat jaya vighnam mahā yantram iti kṛtvā sa dānavaḥ nismṛtya nagarāt bhūyastriṃśat akṣauhiṇī vṛtaḥ punar daityaḥ viśukraḥ kaṭakam dviṣām aśrūyanta tatas tasya raṇa niḥsāṇa nisvanāḥ tathā api tāḥ nirudyogāḥ śaktayaḥ kaṭake abhavan a spṛṣṭe mantriṇī daṇḍanāthe cintām avā patuḥ kasya vā atha vikāreṇa sainikāḥ nirgata udyamāḥ nirasta āyudha saṃrambhāḥ nidrā tandrā vighūrṇitāḥ na mānayanti vākyāni rārcayanti maheśvarīm audāsīnyam vitanvanti śaktayaḥ nispṛhāḥ imāḥ iti te mantriṇī daṇḍanāthe cintā parāyaṇe cakra syandanam ārūḍhe mahā rājñīm samūcatuḥ uvāca na śṛṇvanti mahā rājñi te ājñām viśva pālitām kā daṇḍinī mantriṇī kā mahā rājñī iti kā punar yuddham ca kīdṛśam iti kṣepam bhūri vitanvate atra yat prāptarūpam tat mahā rājñi prapadyatām iti uktvā saha daṇḍinyā mantriṇī praṇatim vyadhāt tatas sā lalitā devī kāmeśvara mukham prati samahasat ati rakta rada āvaliḥ tasyāḥ smita prabhā puñje kuñjara ākṛtimān mukhe kaṭa kroḍa galat dānaḥ kaścid eva vyajṛṃbhata japā paṭala pāṭalyaḥ bāla candra vapus dharaḥ bījapūra gadām ikṣu cāpam śūlam sudarśanam abja pāśa utpala vrīhimañjarī varadām kuśān tundilaḥ candra cūḍālaḥ mandra bṛṃhita nisvanaḥ siddhi lakṣmī samāśliṣṭaḥ praṇanāma maheśvarīm tayā kṛta āśīḥ sa mahān gaṇanāthaḥ gajānanaḥ pṛṣṭhāt cūrmīkaroti sma jaya vighna mahā śilām tatra sthitābhiḥ duṣṭābhiḥ devatābhiḥ saha eva saḥ parāga śeṣa tām nītvā tat yantram prakṣipat divi tatas kilakilā rāvam kṛtvā ālasya vivarjitāḥ udyatāḥ samaram kartum śaktayaḥ śastra pāṇayaḥ sa deti vadanaḥ kaṇṭha kalita akuṇṭha nisvanaḥ jaya yantram hi tat sṛṣṭam tathā rātrau vyanāśayat imam vṛttāntam ākarṇya bhaṇḍaḥ sa kṣobham āyayau bahūn ātma rūpān dantāvala ānanān cañcarīka kulaiḥ agre gīyamāna mahā udayāḥ sphurat dāḍima kiñjalka vikṣepa kara rociṣaḥ sadā ratna ākara aneka helayā pātum udyatāḥ āmoda pramukhāḥ ṛddhi mukhya śakti niṣevitāḥ ari ghnaḥ vighna karttā ca ṣaṭ ete vighna nāyakāḥ te sapta koṭi saṃkhyānām herambāṇām adhīśvarāḥ agni prākāra valayāt vinirgatya gaja ānanāḥ punar pracaṇḍa phūtkāra badhirīkṛta viṣṭapāḥ papāta daitya sainyeṣu gaṇa cakra camū gaṇaḥ taiḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ gaṇanāthaḥ sa dānavān gaṇanāthena tasya abhūt viśukrasya mahā ojasaḥ bhrukuṭī kuṭile cakre daṣṭa uṣṭham ati pāṭalam mad āghaṭṭana nisvānaiḥ huṃkāraiḥ ca suradviṣām daitya sapti khura krīḍat kuddāla kūṭa nisvanaiḥ phetkāraiḥ ca bhayena ākrandanaiḥ api dhanuṣām guṇa nissvānaiḥ cakra cītkaraṇaiḥ api śara sātkāra ghoṣaiḥ ca vīra bhāṣā kadambakaiḥ aṭṭahāsaiḥ mahā indrāṇām siṃhanādaiḥ ca bhūriśas triṃśat akṣauhiṇī senā viśukrasya durātmanaḥ pratyekam yodhayāḥ māsuḥ gaṇanāthāḥ mahā rathāḥ dantaiḥ marma vibhindantaḥ viṣṭaṃyataḥ ca śuṇḍayā krodhayantaḥ karṇa tālaiḥ puṣkala āvartaka upamaiḥ nāsā śvāsaiḥ ca paruṣaiḥ vikṣipantaḥ patākinīm piṃṣantaḥ ca pada āghātaiḥ pīnaiḥ ghnantaḥ tathā udaraiḥ vibhindantaḥ ca śūlena kṛttantaḥ cakra pātanaiḥ śaṅkha svanena mahatā trāsayantaḥ varūthinīm gaṇanātha mukha udbhūtāḥ gaja vakrāḥ sahasraśas dhūli śeṣam samastam tat sainyam cakruḥ mahā udyatāḥ sapta akṣauhiṇī yuktena yuyudhe sa gaṇeśvaraḥ samālokya gaja asura bhujā balam vardhamānam ca tat vīryam viśukraḥ prapalāyitaḥ sapta akṣauhiṇikā yuktam gaja asuram amardayat kālarātriḥ ca daityānām sā rātriḥ viratim gatā lalitā ca ati muditā babhūva asya parākramaiḥ vitatāra mahā rājñī prīyamāṇā gaṇeśituḥ sarva daivata pūjāyāḥ pūrva pūjya tvam uttamam iti śrī brahmāṇḍapurāṇe uttara bhāge hayagrīva agastya saṃvāde lalita upākhyāne gaṇanāthaparākramaḥ nāma saptaviṃśaḥ adhyāyaḥ mahā daityam bhaṇḍa daityaḥ sahodaram senānām kadanam śrutvā santaptaḥ bahu cintayā preṣayāmāsa yuddhāya bhaṇḍa daityaḥ sahodarau viṣaṅgaḥ ca viśukraḥ ca mahodyama mavāpanuḥ kaniṣṭha sahitam tatra yuvarājam mahā balam senānām āvṛtaḥ ca saḥ yuvarājaḥ pravavṛdhe pratāpena mahīyasā ulūkajit prabhṛtayaḥ bhāgineyāḥ daśa uddhatāḥ bhaṇḍasya ca bhaginyām tu dhūminyām jāta yonayaḥ kṛta astra śikṣāḥ bhaṇḍena mātulena mahīyasā dvayoḥ mātulayoḥ prītim bhāgineyāḥ vitenire ārūḍha yānāḥ pratyeka gāḍha ahaṅkāra śālinaḥ ākṛṣṭa guru dhanvānaḥ viśukram anuvavrajuḥ bhīta vāraṇaḥ prāpa viśukraḥ yuddha medinīm tatas kalakala ārāva kāriṇyā senayā vṛtaḥ viśukraḥ paṭu dadhvāna siṃhanādam bhayaṃkaram tad kṣobhāt kṣubhita svāntāḥ śaktayaḥ saṃbhrama uddhatāḥ taḍit mayam iva ākāśam kurvantyaḥ sva sva rociṣā rakta amvuja āvṛtam iva vyoma cakram raṇa unmukhāḥ atha bhaṇḍaka nīyāṃsau āgatau yuddha durmadau niśamya yugapad yoddham mantriṇī daṇḍa nāyake miricakam jñeya cakram ārūḍhe ratha śekharam dhṛta ātapatra valaye cāmarābhyām ca vījite nirjagamatuḥ raṇam kartum ubhābhyām lalitā ājñayā śrī cakraratha rājasya rakṣaṇa artham niveśite śata akṣauhiṇikām senām varjayitvā astra bhīṣaṇam anyat sarvam camu jālam nirjagāma raṇa unmukhī puratas prācalat daṇḍanāthā ratha niṣedivāḥ ekayā eva kara aṅgulyā ghūrṇayantī halāyudham tarala indu kalā cūḍā sphurat potra mukha ambujā dhanuṣaḥ dhvaninā viśvam pūrayantī mahā uddhatā pāṇinā padma ramyeṇa maṇi kaṅkaṇa cāruṇā tūṇīra mukhataḥ kṛṣṭam bhrāmayantī śilīmukham dārayantī kṣiti talam daityānām hṛdayaiḥ saha loka atiśāyi tā viśva manaḥ mohana kāriṇā akṣauhiṇī sahasrāṇām aṣṭakam samara uddhatam karṣatī kalpa viśleṣa nirmaryāda abdhi saṃnibham tasyāḥ śakti camū cakre kāścid kanaka rociṣaḥ kāścid dāḍima saṃkāśāḥ kāścid jīmūta rociṣaḥ anyāḥ sindūra rucayaḥ parāḥ pāṭala pāṭalāḥ kāca adrikā ambarāḥ kāścid parāḥ śyāmala komalāḥ anyāḥ tu hīraka prakhyāḥ parāḥ gārutmata upamāḥ viruddhaiḥ pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ miśritaiḥ śata koṭibhiḥ asaṃkhyāḥ śaktayaḥ celuḥ daṇḍinyāḥ sainike tathā yathā bhūṣaṇa veṣa ādi yathā prabhāva lakṣaṇam yathā sat guṇa śāli tvam yathā ca āśrita lakṣaṇam yathā daitya ogha saṃhāraḥ yathā sarvaiḥ ca pūjitā yathā śaktiḥ mahā rājñyāḥ deḍinyaḥ ca tathā akhilam mahā rājñī vitīrṇam tad ājñā mudrā aṅgulīyakam ittham pracalite sainye mantriṇī daṇḍanāthayoḥ tad bhāra bhaṅgurā bhūmiḥ delā līlām alaṃbata tatas pravavṛte yuddham tumulam roma harṣaṇam uddhūta dhūli jambālībhūta saptārṇavī jalam mādhoraṇaiḥ hastipakāḥ khaḍgaiḥ padgāḥ ca saṅga tāḥ daṇḍa nātha viṣaṅgeṇa samayudhyanta saṅgare mahā śukreṇa samam śyāmā vikṛṣṭa maṇi kārmukā aśva rūḍhā cakāra uccais saha ulūkajitā raṇam sampad īśāḥ ca jagrāha puruṣeṇa yuyutsayā viṣeṇa nakulī devī samāhvāsta yuyutsayā kuntiṣeṇena samaram mahā māyā tadā akarot laghuśyāmā cakāra uccais kuśūreṇa samam raṇam svapneśī maṅgala ākhyena daitya indreṇa raṇam vyadhāt vāgvādinī tu jaghaṭe drughaṇena samam raṇe kolāṭena ca duṣṭena caṇḍa kālī akarot raṇam akṣauhiṇībhiḥ daityānām śata akṣauhiṇikāḥ tathā pravartamāne samare viśukraḥ duṣṭa dānavaḥ vardhamānām śakti camūm hīyamānām nijām camūm avalokya ruṣā āviṣṭaḥ sa kṛṣṭa guru kārmukaḥ tena dāva anala jvālā dīptena mathitam balam ha viśukra mukta tarṣa astra vyākulāḥ śaktayaḥ avan kṣobhayan indriya grāmam tālu mūlam viśoṣayan pātayan pṛthivī pṛṣṭhe deham visraṃsita āyudham āvirbabhūva śaktīnām ati tīvraḥ tṛṣā jvaraḥ mantriṇī saha potriṇyā bhṛśam cintām avāpa ha uvāca tām daṇḍanāthām atyāhita viśaṅkinīm sakhi potriṇi duṣṭasya tarṣa astram idam āgatam śithilīkurute sainyam asmākam hā vidheḥ kramaḥ viśuṣka tālu mūlānām vibhraṣṭa āyudha tejasām śaktīnām maṇḍalena atra samare samupekṣitam viśuṣka tālu
